*Introduction
These interpretations have been written to introduce you to the concepts of astrology and how to get started with your natal chart. Astrology is a complex and meaningful science which takes years to study and apply successfully, however, we would like to whet your appetite with this report from this program, and encourage you to deepen your understanding through other means.
|
|Astrology is a study of the connection between planets and life on Earth. It is based on a concept that energy patterns form between other planets and Earth; and that these energies affect our lives as individuals and communities.
|
|An astrological chart, also known as a horoscope, natal chart, or birth chart, records the relationship between the planets and the signs of the Zodiac. Charts can be calculated for the birth of a person, a community, an event or anything that seems momentous. The horoscope is as individual and unique as a fingerprint.
|
|When using these interpretations, please bear in mind that, inevitably, every chart will contain some contradictory influences, and as a result certain interpretations of different items in the same chart may seem difficult to reconcile. However, this may still be an accurate reflection of your chart, as it is likely that you do experience conflicting desires, events and circumstances in your life. Usually it is the responsibility of an astrologer to synthesise these apparent contradictions in order to present a cohesive and realistic interpretation of the dilemmas of the chart.
|
|This text has been written by astrologer Stephanie Johnson.
|
|If you would like further information about your birth chart please visit www.seeingwithstars.net

;*DynamicAspects



*Aspect Conjunction Conjunction
Angle 0 Degrees 
|Any Harmonic. 
|This aspect emphasises and fuses the energies of the planets involved. Each planet modifies or strengthens the other. The activities are focussed and intensified.

*Aspect Opposition Opposition
Angle 180 Degrees 
|2nd, 4th, 6th, 8th, 10th, 12th Harmonic. 
|This aspect depicts conflict which, when resolved, results in growth. Oppositions show a tug of war between opposing forces. If they are resolved, then the oppositions become the backbone and strength of the chart.

*Aspect Trine Trine
Angle 120 Degrees 
|3rd, 6th, 9th, 12th Harmonic. 
|This aspect shows an easy flow of energy and is generally considered favorable. You will mostly experience trines as talents and advantageous. However, trines can also show areas which are the line of least resistance. This means that you may be letting these talents slip by unnoticed and that you are lacking motivation.

*Aspect Square Square
Angle 90 Degrees 
|4th, 8th, 12th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is a seat of inner tensions. The tension of the square gives our motivation. Squares are dynamic aspects which give us the drive to succeed. What begins as an inner problem is overcome or accepted, and then becomes a door to understanding.

*Aspect Sextile Sextile
Angle 60 Degrees 
|6th, 12th Harmonic. 
|This is an easy aspect showing co-operation between two planets which leads to opportunity. It has a positive blending effect on the planets.

*Aspect Semisquare Semisquare
Angle 45 Degrees 
|8th Harmonic. 
|This aspect shows areas of inflexibility - obstacles that stand in the way of our changing and adapting to circumstances. These can cause irritation. This aspect is calling for either great persistence or for an alternative approach to bypass the problem.

*Aspect Sesquisquare Sesquisquare
Angle 135 Degrees 
|8th Harmonic. 
|This aspect (also known as a sesquiquadrate) shows areas of frustration that are likely to be blown out of proportion.  We are likely to react with resentment and impatience. The lesson is to develop patience and persistence.

*Aspect Semisextile
Angle 30 Degrees 
|12th Harmonic. 
|This aspect shows us opportunities which are available in our lives but, which may slip by unnoticed. We are being asked to take up the opportunity.

*Aspect Quincunx Quincunx
Angle 150 Degrees 
|12th Harmonic. 
|This aspect (also known as an inconjunct) shows areas which are difficult to integrate. The quincunx is calling for a change or adjustment in order to make the most of the areas affected.

*Aspect Quintile
Angle 72 Degrees 
|5th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered a creative one. It indicates talent and creativity that flows easily.

*Aspect BiQuintile
Angle 144 Degrees 
|5th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered a creative one. Like the Quintile it indicates talent and creativity that flows easily.

*Aspect Decile
Angle 36 Degrees 
|10th Harmonic. 
|Also known as the Semi-Quintile this aspect is said to indicate the ability to help others achieve their dreams.

*Aspect SesquiQuintile
Angle 108 Degrees 
|10th Harmonic. 
|Also known as the Tridecile this aspect is said to indicate the a need for introspection in order to achieve creative outcomes.

*Aspect Septile
Angle 51.428571 Degrees 
|7th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered a creative one, but only after effort. It indicates talent and creativity that flows as a result of conflict. It can indicate productivity but only once work has been done or as a result of friction.

*Aspect BiSeptile
Angle 102.857143 Degrees 
|7th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered a creative one, but only after effort. Like the Septile it indicates talent and creativity that flows as a result of hard work. It can indicate productivity but only once work has been done or as a result of friction.

*Aspect TriSeptile
Angle 154.285714 Degrees 
|7th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered a creative one, but only after effort. Like the Septile it indicates talent and creativity that flows as a result of hard work. It can indicate productivity but only once work has been done or as a result of friction.

*Aspect Novile
Angle 40 Degrees 
|9th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered to indicate learning about oneself through relationship with others and the universe. It is considered a profound angle and is often used in relationship astrology.

*Aspect BiNovile
Angle 80 Degrees 
|9th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered to indicate learning about oneself through relationship with others and the universe.

*Aspect QuadriNovile
Angle 160 Degrees 
|9th Harmonic. 
|This aspect is considered to indicate learning about oneself through relationship with others and the universe.

*Aspect Parallel
The Parallel refers to degrees of declination above or below the ecliptic. It is considered a strong positive influence.
|

*Aspect ContraParallel
The Contraparallel (or Antiparallel) is an aspect which refers to degrees of declination above or below the ecliptic. It is said to be similar to a weak Opposition.

; Quadrant Interpretations

*Quadrant 1 
This quadrant begins at the 1st House cusp and ends at the 4th. It refers to the development of self-identity. When this quadrant is highlighted it indicates your need to pursue self-interests. This quadrant outlines a need for self-development and self-concern.

*Quadrant 1 Strong
You see yourself as an independent individual, capable of organising your own life. You could be self-centred. The planets in this quadrant will highlight the areas of life in which you want to express yourself.

*Quadrant 2 
This quadrant begins at the 4th House cusp and ends at the 7th. It refers to the person's need for inner security and relationships with others. This quadrant points to an awareness of other people.

*Quadrant 2 Strong
You are receptive to other people and sensitive to the undercurrents involved in relationships.

*Quadrant 3 
This quadrant begins at the 7th House cusp and ends at the 10th. It refers to worldly issues and relationships. When this quadrant is highlighted it indicates that you focus on others more than on yourself. You need to relate to society, putting others before your own needs.

*Quadrant 3 Strong
You will look for relationships with an objective, rather than personal, outlook. You also want to be public, and to play your part in society.

*Quadrant 4 
This quadrant begins at the 10th House and ends at the 1st. It refers to personal efforts which contribute to humanity. This quadrant outlines the need to be focused on the goal of public service. It also means that you are likely to be a more private person, concentrating on home, family or matters of a private nature.

*Quadrant 4 Strong
You strive to make your mark on the world. This may be beneficial, but could become disruptive if you become too caught up in an ideal.

; Hemisphere Interpretations

*Hemisphere Eastern 
This hemisphere is on the left of the chart, spanning the 10th house through to the 3rd house.

*Hemisphere Eastern Strong
You are a self-motivated and self-oriented individual. You like to map out your own life and follow your own path, experiencing difficulties only if anyone stands in your way. You value your independence and enjoy your own company. You enjoy the company of other people, but only if they give you plenty of freedom for your own pursuits. You need to watch out for egocentric and selfish behaviour.

*Hemisphere Northern 
This hemisphere is on the bottom of the chart, spanning the 1st house through to the 6th house.

*Hemisphere Northern Strong
Your identity and personal resources are the basis of all other success in your life. You need to feel secure within yourself before you step out into the world. Family roots and your home environment will provide the foundations for self- discovery and self-knowledge that will form the foundation for future success. You need to make sure that you do not become a stay-at-home.

*Hemisphere Western 
This hemisphere is on the right of the chart, spanning the 4th house through to the 9th house.

*Hemisphere Western Strong
Your interactions with other people take on a paramount role in your life. You value both your personal relationships, and the interactions of the human race. You have a gift for mediating in your relationships, as you possess insight into the nuances of relationships. You learn most about yourself in the context of your relationships. You need to make sure you are not engulfed in stifling relationships.

*Hemisphere Southern 
This hemisphere is on the top of the chart, spanning the 7th house through to the 12th house.

*Hemisphere Southern Strong
Public life is the pinnacle for you. You gain personal satisfaction from your achievements in the world, and learn much about yourself through your position in the public arena. Your need for a high public profile could be met through both your career and your social status. You need to make sure that your achievements are not at the expense of your loved ones.

; Element Interpretations

*Element Fire 
Fire is a Yang or Masculine element. It denotes enthusiasm, dynamism, spontaneity, and the lack of reflection.

*Element Fire Weak
You have difficulty getting yourself motivated to achieve your own goals. In fact at times you may lack the self-confidence to even set personal goals. You may experience a general lack of enthusiasm, feeling overwhelmed by change.

*Element Fire Strong
You are a highly-motivated person with many goals and aspirations for the future. You are vital and spontaneous, often enjoying the challenge of travelling down new and adventurous roads in your life. Your enthusiasm is irrepressible. Your weakness lies in your tendency to exaggerate and your inability to cope with the more mundane activities in life.

*Element Earth 
Earth is a Yin or Feminine element. It denotes reliability, stability, solidity, stoicism, sensuality, and practicality.

*Element Earth Weak
You have difficulty coping with the realities of every day life. Practical daily chores seem beyond your capabilities, and you have difficulty concentrating on matters at hand.

*Element Earth Strong
You are a practical and efficient, hands-on person. You can be relied on to take a common-sense approach to most matters. Your down-to-earth manner stands you in good stead for the daily chores of life. Your weakness lies in your sometimes stubborn refusal to make changes in your life. You tend to stifle both your own and other people's enthusiasm.

*Element Air 
Air is a Yang or Masculine element. It denotes communication, talking, writing, thinking, intellect, a quick flow of ideas.

*Element Air Weak
You lack objectivity - the ability to stand back and view aspects of life from a detached and rational perspective. You have difficulty making decisions and in the process of weighing up the pros and cons in a logical manner.

*Element Air Strong
You are objective and philosophical, preferring to view life from an intellectual perspective. Your rational mind will outweigh your feelings every time, as you consider the world of emotions to be irrational. You have a high sense of fairness, and a logical thought process. Your weakness lies in the fact that you view emotions in a disparaging light.

*Element Water 
Water is a Yin or Feminine element. It denotes emotions, nurturance, security, caring, and comfort.

*Element Water Weak
You are out of kilter with your emotions. Crying or losing your cool in front of other people would be a horrifying thought, let alone action, for you. You often lack compassion for others in your human relationships, and need to learn to honor both your own and other people's feelings.

*Element Water Strong
You speak from your heart, and are a compassionate and caring person with a strong intuitional nature. You value your personal relationships, in which you often taking on a caretaker role. You are such a sympathetic and understanding person that you are often caught in the role of mother to your loved ones. Your weakness lies in the fact that you fail to take an objective perspective when necessary. You often react without thinking things through first.

; Mode Interpretations

*Mode Cardinal 
The Cardinal signs are: Aries, Cancer, Libra, and Capricorn. Cardinal denotes wanting to express energy actively and seeking challenge. The basic essence of cardinal signs is survival.

*Mode Cardinal Weak
You prefer to follow in other people's footsteps rather than initiate actions. You can be relied on to come up with the goods as long as someone else has the initial ideas. Your survival mechanisms are weak.

*Mode Cardinal Strong
You enjoy challenge and action, and become frustrated when you have no recourse for change. You expect others to also rise to a challenge.

*Mode Fixed 
The Fixed signs are: Leo, Scorpio, Aquarius and Taurus. Fixed denotes wanting to remain stable and security. The basic essence of fixed signs is growth.

*Mode Fixed Weak
You like to flit from one thing to another, finding difficult to settle down. You enjoy change, although you lack the stability needed to see things through.

*Mode Fixed Strong
You do not enjoy change. You expect others to be reliable, like yourself.

*Mode Mutable 
The Mutable signs are: Sagittarius, Pisces, Gemini and Virgo. Mutable denotes wanting to be flexible and adaptable. The basic essence of mutable signs is adaptability.

*Mode Mutable Weak
You find it difficult to adapt to new situations. You tend to be inflexible when faced with the demands of change and other people.

*Mode Mutable Strong
You may procrastinate. You expect others to be flexible, like yourself.

; Ray Interpretations

*Ray 1 
Will and power

*Ray 1 Strong
You can be powerful, assertive and persistent. You have a strong sense of purpose, and have the ability to lead, direct and govern. However, you may have a tendency towards excessive pride, hunger for power and obstinacy.

*Ray 2 
Love and wisdom

*Ray 2 Strong
You can be wise, loving and compassionate. You have a strong sensitivity to others and have patience and tact. However, you may have a tendency towards self-pity, over-sensitivity, fearfulness and lack of assertiveness.

*Ray 3 
Active intelligence and adaptability

*Ray 3 Strong
You can be clever, mentally agile and strategizing. You are a skilful communicator, have a good business sense and a capacity for abstract  thinking. However, you may have a tendency towards intellectual pride, deviousness and restlessness.

*Ray 4 
Harmony through conflict

*Ray 4 Strong
You can be spontaneous, imaginative and conciliating. You have a love of beauty and music, and the ability to reconcile opposites. However, you may have a tendency to worry, be moody, combative and indecisive.

*Ray 5 
Concrete knowledge and science

*Ray 5 Strong
You can be focused, objective and keenly inquisitive. You are an expert in your chosen field, enjoy verifying through experimentation, and have a practical inventiveness. However, you may have a tendency towards over-rationalisation, excessive scepticism and criticism, and lack of emotional responsiveness.

*Ray 6 
Devotion and idealism

*Ray 6 Strong
You can be enthusiastic, loyal and devoted. You have strong idealism and humility the ability to inspire others. However, you may have a tendency towards fanaticism, gullibility, rigid idealism and over-emotionalism.

*Ray 7 
Ceremonial order and magic

*Ray 7 Strong
You can be well-organised, socially aware and refined. You have a good sense of timing, an ability to build things and attend to details. However, you may have a tendency towards over- regimentation, perfectionism, materialism and over-concern with rules.

; Lunar Phase Interpretations

*Phase NewMoon
Moon 0 to 45 degrees ahead of the Sun. 
|You are an impulsive person, always looking for new opportunities to express your ideas. You react from your own subjective viewpoint. You enjoy starting new projects.

*Phase Crescent
Moon 45 to 90 degrees ahead of the Sun. 
|You are an assertive person, eager to leave behind the past and get on with the future. You usually have faith in your own abilities to rise to challenges.

*Phase FirstQuarter
Moon from 90 to 135 degrees ahead of the Sun. 
|You are an action oriented person with managerial capabilities and the ability to get results. You may sometimes push too hard for your ideals.

*Phase Gibbous
Moon 135 to 180 degrees ahead of the Sun. 
|You are a resourceful and goal-oriented person seeking purpose and meaning in your life. You can often be found seeking knowledge to add value to your life.

*Phase FullMoon
Moon 180 to 135 degrees behind the Sun. 
|You are concerned mainly with the nature of relationships. Your concern is not limited to personal relationships, but relationships of all kinds. Hence relationships will feature prominently in your own life.

*Phase Disseminating
Moon 135 to 90 degrees behind the Sun. 
|Sharing your knowledge with the world is a major motivation in your life. You believe you have gained much knowledge and wisdom through your experiences, and want to ensure others have the benefit.

*Phase ThirdQuarter
Moon from 90 to 45 degrees behind the Sun. 
|You have strong beliefs and are likely to put them into action. You usually have the wisdom to know when to act, but sometimes can be inflexible.

*Phase Balsamic
Moon less than 45 degrees behind the Sun. 
|You are a future-oriented person. You feel destiny plays a large part in your life, and may have some gifts in prophecy and leadership.

; Point Interpretations

*Moon
Astrologically, the Moon gives vital information about your feelings and basic needs.  What do you need to feel good in life? What do you enjoy? Are you successful in fulfilling these needs and experiencing enjoyment as an adult? And did you get these needs met at a young age? Did you enjoy your childhood? These are a few of the questions answered in your chart by the Moon. Information about your mother or major caregiver can also be gleaned from this luminary, as your relationship with your mother is closely linked with the satisfaction of your basic needs.

*Earth
The position of the Earth is used more commonly in Esoteric Astrology or Heliocentric Astrology. In Esoteric Astrology it is considered to represent our point on the spiritual path. It is the point at which you need to make physical your spiritual potential; literally what your next physical step is, on the spiritual path. It represents your dharma.

*Sun
The Sun is one of the luminaries and it is said to represent your personality - how you express yourself in the world. Do you express yourself well? Do you really shine in your life or do you struggle to shine?  The Sun can also give you information about your relationship with your father.

*Vulcan
Vulcan is more commonly used in the field of Esoteric Astrology. It has yet to be officially discovered and therefore its position is still open to speculation. Esoteric Astrologers believe that Vulcan is a powerful planet and will be discovered only when humanity is ready to use its tremendous power. It represents the power to smash or breakdown crystallised matter and form, to pave the way for the fusion of new forms. Its speculative position shows where you need to break down the old in order to forge the new.

*Mercury
Mercury stands for the intellect, common sense, cold reason, commerce and business. Its qualities are fluidity and versatility. Its position and aspects tell you about your communication and learning habits and your modes of thinking.

*Venus
Venus is the planet which reveals how you like to relate to your environment and to other people. This planet is one of the key points in your chart examined by an astrologer when you ask about your relationships. Venus reveals the type of person to whom you are attracted and your expectations of relationships. It shows what gives you pleasure.

*Mars
Mars is the planet of assertion and drive. What drives you? Do you pursue your desires aggressively or do you sit back, lacking confidence? This planet tells you what motivates you and what desires drive you most powerfully.

*Jupiter
Jupiter is the planet of expansion, abundance and wisdom. It highlights the areas in which you yearn to discover greater truths. Therefore it can also be linked to excess. You search for more and more insofar as you can learn greater truths. It is the seeker. In seeking you find.

*Saturn
Saturn represents responsibility, boundaries and structure; structure that provides a positive framework within which you can build, or structure that limits your development and forces you to reassess your liabilities and assets.

*Uranus
Uranus represents originality and unconventionality. This can be both the unusual and brilliant genius or the wilful rebel without a cause. It tells you the areas in which you break with convention, become innovative and experiment with new and exciting ways.

*Neptune
Neptune is the planet of mysticism and at-one-ness. It represents both the blissful at-one-ment of the spiritual and the confusion which comes from not knowing limits and boundaries. It blurs reality and fantasy and teaches you compassion and unity.

*Pluto
Pluto is the planet of transformation. Nothing stays the same around this planet. Its task is to clear out the old to make way for the new. This is done volcanically, by forcing anything submerged to the surface to be dispelled. Wherever Pluto sits in your chart you experience regeneration.

*Chiron
Chiron, the Wounded Healer, represents your emotional and physical wounds. It reveals a part of you that is hurt, small and vulnerable. You are encouraged to heal your wounds, and then look beyond personal realms, to see the suffering of others, and to become a teacher or healer.

*Vesta
Vesta represents the issue of commitment. This includes commitment to work and to relationships. Where does your commitment lie?  Where are you focusing your energies?

*Pallas
Pallas tells of how you perceive things, your creative intelligence. It is more mental than emotional. It reveals your capacity for original thought. Do you have artistic ability?  How do you express your mental creativity?

*Juno
Juno is the asteroid of right relations within marriage. It tells of issues of fairness and unfairness within the marriage partnership. It also reveals the capacity for committed relationships.

*Ceres
Ceres represents nurturing. Therefore it reveals information about the mother-child relationship. It is how you nurture others and how you need to be nurtured. It also tells of your capacity to love yourself and others unconditionally.

*Hygeia
Hygeia tells us of health issues. It ranges from quite simply your state of health to the lessons you do or don't learn from this state.

*Astraea
Astraea represents the inability to let go. It points to blockages that stop you seeing when something is over or finished, ready for something new to begin.

*NorthNode
The North Node points to a key lesson in your life. It represents new experiences towards which you must aim during this life. You have already learnt the skills of its opposite point, the South Node, in past lives. Now you must grow and stretch yourself through the lessons of the North Node. The challenge with the Nodal Axis is to use the past skills of the South Node and learn the new skills of the North Node on your quest for wholeness.

*SouthNode
The South Node represents past life skills and achievements which stand you in good stead for this life. You need to use these skills in the present life to learn the lessons of the opposite point, the North Node. You must not continue to fall back on the past. The challenge with the Nodal Axis is to use the past skills of the South Node and learn the new skills of the North Node on your quest for wholeness.

*Ascendant
The Ascendant or Rising Sign is a key to self-discovery. It tells you how you express yourself as an individual. It is not so much your identity as how you choose to express that identity. The older you get, the more you strive to express yourself through the qualities of the Ascendant. In contrast, the Descendant tells of qualities you attract in relationships. The Descendant qualities often appear in your most intimate partners as signposts to lessons about yourself. Both ends of the polarity give you clues about you as a person, and how you relate to others.

*Midheaven
The MC or Medium Coeli tells us of your public life. This includes your social status, in particular your marital state and your chosen profession. It can also show how you crave recognition.

*Vertex
The Vertex is the point where the Prime Vertical intersects the Ecliptic in the west. The opposite point, in the east is called the Antivertex. The Vertex axis describes a point of awareness that opens doorways to other realities.  It can remain a dormant energy in the chart and not responsive to zodiac and planetary energies until it is the right time for it to awaken.   When it does awaken, it describes a process of enlightenment that takes you beyond mundane life.   It is an angle that gives a profound understanding of the nature of the sign and house in which it resides and the planets that are in aspect. 

*EastPoint
The East Point is the point where the eastern horizon intersects the Prime Vertical and the Celestial Equator. It is sometimes thought to be somewhat similar to the Ascendant.

*PartofFortune
The Part of Fortune represents your opportunities for spiritual integration. Therefore it often points to how you experience joy; the joy that comes with union with the soul or higher self.

*Cupido
Cupido is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents the arts and beauty, relationships, family, family history, marriage, and sociability.

*Hades
Hades is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents suffering, loneliness, poverty, deteriorisation, drudgery, depressing emotions and compassion.

*Zeus
Zeus is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents purposeful activity, enthusiasm, creative energy,  machines, and weapons.

*Kronos
Kronos is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents authority, leadership, mastery, differences of opinion, and bureaucracy.

*Apollon
Apollon is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents career opportunities, overseas connections, and multiple interests.

*Admetos
Admetus is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents delays, frustrations, complications, endurance and perseverance.

*Vulcanus
Vulcanus is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents power, compulsion, forging bonds, and fate.

*Poseidon
Poseidon is one of the Trans-Neptunian Planets. It represents spiritual influences, religion, ethics, and enlightenment.

*TransPluto
TransPluto is a hypothetical planet, which is said to orbit beyond Pluto.  It is often referred to as Persephone. When in a prominent position in your birth charts TransPluto describes an early childhood environment where you felt criticised, forced to comply with the expectations of others and unable to develop your inner self. Astrologers say that it triggers a desire for perfection that results in an over concern with what others think.

*BlackMoon
This sensitive point represents the darker side of your nature, characteristics you know exist and need to address, but prefer not to acknowledge. The Sign of her placement and the condition of the Ruling Planet, will determine the way in which the Black Moon expresses herself in your birth chart. The Astrological House she occupies describes an area of life in which you can become aware of this dark side and examine aspects of yourself, which you deny and often project onto others. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok.
|

*CoAscendant
The Co-Ascendant and Co-Descendant are sensitive points, best viewed as a pair of points, which lie across a chart axis. Unlike the Ascendant which represents the physical body the Co Ascendant is thought to be associated with non-sensory connections that you make with others. It describes non-sensory input, impressions obtained from those around the individual, which have no basis in the five physical senses.
|

*PolarAscendant
The Polar Ascendant and Descendant are considered to be personal sensitive points, best viewed as a pair, which lie across a chart axis. 

*Descendant
The Descendant tells of qualities we attract in relationships. These qualities appear in our most intimate partners and yet are signposts to lessons that we need to learn about ourselves. The Descendant also reflects business partnerships and contracts. The Descendant is part of an axis formed with the Ascendant or Rising Sign. Both ends of the polarity give us clues about our selves. In contrast, the Ascendant is a key to self-discovery. It tells us how we express ourselves as individuals. It is not so much our identity as how we choose to express that identity. The older we get, the more we strive to express ourselves through the qualities of the Ascendant.

*Imum Coeli
Imum  Coeli literally meaning "bottom the sky" in Latin is the point directly opposite the Midheaven  Also known as the IC It marks the cusp of the fourth house in some house systems. The IC represents the foundations, parental influences (particularly father), the childhood home and early experiences. It can also represent endings.

*EquatorialDescendant
Sometimes incorrectly referred to as the East Point, the Equatorial Ascendant is the point where the Earth's equator intercepts the ecliptic.  In a natal chart it is the degree that would have been ascending if the person had been born on the Equator. It is not one point but one of a pair of points, which lie across a chart axis and therefore should be delineated together.  While these points may not be commonly used, some astrologers view them as an secondary ascendant/descendant which gives them extra information as to how you approach personal relationships and activities. Often in the same sign as the Ascendant it can fall in the 12th or 1st house, giving another dimension as to its expression.  

*CoDescendant
The Co-Ascendant and Co-Descendant are sensitive points, best viewed as a pair of points, which lie across a chart axis. Unlike the Ascendant which represents the physical body the Co Ascendant is thought to be associated with non-sensory connections that you make with others. It describes non-sensory input, impressions obtained from those around the individual, which have no basis in the five physical senses.

*PolarDescendant
The Polar Ascendant and Descendant are considered to be personal sensitive points, best viewed as a pair, which lie across a chart axis. 

*AriesPoint
The Aries Point  indicates an bring things forward and out. It relates to your potential to initiate matters.

*WhiteMoon
Selena or the White Moon is a hypothetical second Moon of the Earth moving about the Earth in seven years. In mythology Selene is the Goddess of the Moon and is often represented as a woman with the crescent moon on her head. The myth talks of her lighting up the night sky as she begins her journey freshly washed in the earth's oceans. Some stories state that she comes down to earth again when she sees and falls in love with a beautiful mortal, bearing him 50 children. Astrologers vary on their interpretation of Selena, however; it is likely that she represents the point of awareness whereby we understand our role on earth and start on our soul's journey, lighting the way for others.

*Sedna
Sedna is a planet-like body located in the coldest known region of our solar system. She was named after the Inuit Goddess of the Sea, who resides in the Arctic underworld and rules over all marine life. Her myth tells of her betrayal by both her father and her husband and her resultant anger which causes violent storms and turbulent seas. Sedna describes where you have the potential to feel powerless. However she also shows you where you can overcome these feelings and play your part in taking care of the planet and humanity.
|

*Eris
Eris is named after the Goddess of strife and discord. She describes adversity and issues of quarrels, rivals, revenge and jealousy. On the other hand the more positive qualities of energy, resourcefulness and the desire to work towards self-improvement are also highlighted by the placement of Eris in your birth chart.

; Point in House Interpretations

*Moon in 1st House
The Moon is placed in the 1st House of your birth chart suggesting that changing fortunes are likely to occur during your lifetime as you seek the stimulation of different homes, professions and environments. You're adaptable and generally enjoy the changes that do occur, as long as you feel that you're moving forward in your life. You're quite ambitious and enjoy being in the limelight, particularly when you feel comfortable in a public situation. Generally you're popular and well-liked because other people respond to your open manner. You're a sensitive person who is affected by the emotions other people, responding with warmth and genuine affection.

*Moon in 2nd House
The Moon is placed in the 2nd House of your birth chart suggesting that you seek emotional security through accruing possessions, although this can be frustrating at times because your personal fortunes have a tendency to fluctuate during your life. Consequently, you face periods of economic insecurity when your fortunes suddenly change. Fortunately
|you've the inner resources to adapt to these changes in income and usually you gain rather than lose money. 
|

*Moon in 3rd House
The Moon is placed in the 3rd House of your birth chart suggesting that you've a strong need to communicate with other people and to keep up with all of the latest news. It doesn't matter if it's the latest gossip about a celebrity or a complex and challenging subject. You have an inquisitive mind and your main aim is to keep up with all that is going on and to expose yourself to new ideas and subjects. You also have a retentive memory and the ability to converse on just about any topic, pulling bits and pieces of information from the recesses of your mind. You also like to express your own ideas to as many people as possible - the more the merrier. For this reason you could enjoy writing, singing or public speaking. You need to find your voice and express yourself, whether in private or in public. Short journeys and changes of environment also appeal giving you more food for thought and satisfying your curiosity.

*Moon in 4th House
The Moon is placed in the 4th House of your birth chart suggesting that your place of residence is constantly undergoing change. This can be that you frequently move home, that your house is constantly in a state of renovation or that the members of your household are often coming and going. Whatever the scenario, it's likely that as a result your home
|doesn't feel secure.  As an adult you may learn to adapt positively to the constant changes in your domestic life, or you may feel a constant
|sense of instability. You've a strong desire to live by the water, and this may provide a sense of deep satisfaction. You could also benefit from working on the land or dealing in property.

*Moon in 5th House
The Moon is placed in the 5th House of your birth chart suggesting that pleasurable pastimes play a prominent role in your life giving you a joie de vivre which is infectious. Sometimes your tendency to play rather than work can stand in the way of you holding down a regular job. Responsibilities simply don't seem to hold the same appeal as play. On a more positive note you're fun-loving and enjoy the company of other people, particularly young people and children. Others respond to your sense of fun and you don't have to look far for company in your playful escapades. You suffer from deeply-buried wounds and moments of overwhelming pain. In exploring the depths of this pain you may later become a catalyst for healing others - a spiritual healer.

*Vesta in 1st House
Your focus is on yourself. This means that you may be selfish and unable to maintain long-term relationships with others. It  also means that you possess the ability to focus on your own self-appointed goals. Your perseverance can lead to great personal achievements.

*Vesta in 2nd House
You are committed to your values. You are also able to focus on providing monetary and physical comfort for yourself and others. You can be tenacious in the pursuit of possessions.

*Vesta in 3rd House

*Vesta in 4th House

*Vesta in 5th House

*Vesta in 6th House
You are committed to serving others. You may also be dedicated to service through healing.

*Vesta in 7th House
Your focus is on intimate relationships. You are dedicated to working on yourself and your role in close relationships, and may become fixated on one important person.

*Vesta in 8th House
You are committed to discovering the mysteries of life. You have the ability to unearth metaphysical truths which you are dedicated to teaching to others. You may experience some difficulties if others are uncomfortable moving beyond the superficial.

*Vesta in 9th House
You are focused on discovering higher truths in life. On the way you may be sidetracked by one or two fanatical belief systems. However in the end you will be committed to sharing your philosophical truths with the world.

*Vesta in 10th House

*Vesta in 11th House
You are dedicated to group processes and to ideals. There is a need for you to define your personal beliefs and visions, but only so that you may persevere in your commitment to your role within the collective.

*Vesta in 12th House
You are committed to a path of spiritual values. You are a dedicated follower of a spiritual way of life. You may delve into the unknown and share your findings with others. You may be committed to working in a spiritual organisation.

*Hygeia in 11th House

*Hygeia in 12th House

*Ascendant in 1st House
The ascendant forms the 1st house cusp in most house systems, so this placement has no particular meaning.

*Midheaven in 10th House
The midheaven forms the 10th house cusp in most house systems, so this placement has no particular meaning.

*Vertex in 1st House
As the Vertex is the point due west of the place of birth and the Ascendant is usually in the East, this position is not likely except at the poles. However, the AntiVertex may function in this capacity.
|This is one of the signatures of a person who has incarnated for a specific destiny. This destiny is connected to either the place of birth or the physical body. This Vertex placement may teach you about the sacredness of your body. You learn of its finely tuned energy system, its chakras and delicate nervous system and learn that you are required to treat it with consideration, love and respect. If you fail to do this then it will fall ill and bring you great pain and limitation. This will be the initiation to stimulate you to develop an understanding of the physical. You spiritual purpose and doorway to higher consciousness is to learn to marry the spiritual with the physical. You may also be required to properly care for your environment, to understand the finely tuned balance of nature and to become part of that harmony.
|The AntiVertex in the 7th House will draw you to people who help you focus and communicate your understanding of this process to the public. The astrological ruler of the Ascendant Conjunct the Vertex axis gives a destined purpose for your life connected to the sign and House of the Vertex placement.

*Vertex in 2nd House
The Vertex in the 2nd House is highly unlikely; however the AntiVertex may function in this capacity. This placement opens the doorway to higher consciousness through learning to value what you have to offer to the world. It is a placement that requires you to regularly assess what you feel are your true values - what is really important to you for quality of life. Money was originally designed to be a fair energy exchange for ideas, goods and labour so the Vertex in this House asks you to be scrupulously fair in all your financial dealings with others. If this is done well you become a focus point for the use of resources and can gain both financially and through status within the community. You may be the custodian of valuable or historical objects - perhaps those passed down the family line, or perhaps owned by the country. You are asked to care for, protect and treasure these items as they may have a purpose in the future. If used ethically and wisely a special talent or vocation will bring considerable financial gain and personal security.
|The AntiVertex in the 8th House draws you to those who have access to research facilities and financial resources that are important to you.

*Vertex in 3rd House
The Vertex in the 3rd House suggests your doorway to higher awareness is connected to skilful communication. Words can be quite magical and sound has been used to stimulate energy points and chakras for many, many centuries. You may find you become interested in the flow of language, story telling, chants, poetry and other forms of the ritual use of words. You could specialise in one of the branches of linguistics, sign language or body language. You may enjoy collecting books and letters from many different people and eras. You delight in their different ways of communication and gain great insight into life through contemplating the variety realities human beings experience.  The birth of your sisters and brothers can have a profound effect on your psyche. It is likely that you have destiny connected to at least one of your siblings. Primary school and the teachers you meet there can strongly affect your life and your approach to learning. The right teacher can teach you how to teach yourself and help you open doors to wonderful worlds of knowledge. As a result you may find you also delight in teaching others.  In one period of your life there will be a short journey or holiday that you can only describe as meant to happen. This can profoundly change you. Choose your cars, boats, bikes and other methods of transport carefully and never be careless with their maintenance. At least one of these methods of transport affects destiny in some way.
|The AntiVertex in the 9th  House draws to you people who broaden your vision and open your eyes to wonderful places in the world. You are destined to know at least one person from a foreign country who deeply influences you.

*Vertex in 4th House
The Vertex in the 4th House gives a profound connection to your country of birth and/or racial origins which deeply influences your way of being. Great insights come through tracing your ancestry and contemplating their lives. You will find at least one ancestor with whom you have considerable affinity as the experiences they had in their life strongly resonates with yours. The Vertex in this position can give a destiny connected to one parent. It may be through their remarkable life, through a strong family resemblance or through intense situations involving this parent. Whichever it is you will find your lives are deeply entwined and there is often the need to finish, or sometimes change for the better, what a parent has started.  Your home is crucially important to your wellbeing as it has a deeply spiritual or even magical affect on you.  Many people with this placement feel as though they are meant to live in a specific area and/or in a specific House. You can search and search for the right abode and know it immediately when you see it, you can move mountains to attain it and feel great relief and peace when you move in. You need to be able to feel connected to the place where you live and able to put down roots for the next generation. 
|The AntiVertex in the 10th  House will draw you to people in positions of administration who can help you attain your goals. You will always be connected to influential people and have at least one destined connection with a powerful person.

*Vertex in 5th House
The Vertex in the 5th House of your Chart indicates your doorway to higher awareness is through love.  This placement can give intense initiations in all matters to do with love.  It can involve children, both your own and those whom are under your care. The initiation is to be able to give love without judgment and learn the difference between 'love' and' like'.  This is a highly creative placement where you are asked to create according to the nature of sign that contains the Vertex. It is often quite difficult to open the door to this creative field, but once you do a whole wider world opens for you as well.  Sport can open the door to a more powerful way of experiencing life. The discipline and commitment required by most forms of sport develop your ability to live life joyfully and successfully.
|The AntiVertex in the 11th House will at times bring friends and groups whom you are destined to have a powerful and sometimes strenuous association.  Your involvement with these people can test your ability to love altruistically and at times to forgive and let go of the past.

*Vertex in 6th House
The Vertex in the 6th House of your Chart indicates your doorway to higher awareness is through service. This placement indicates a test of your ability to be of effective service to others and to value and enjoy what you have to offer. The initiation is to be able to give freely of a specific skill without being at the mercy of other's demands. The service can involve matters of community welfare i.e. police; trade unions; health areas - including natural methods of healing, medicine, physiotherapy, chiropractic, dentistry. You may feel a call to one of these areas that is hard to deny. You will be required to develop a high level of skill in your chosen field. Computers or other forms of machinery that are of service to humankind are also connected to this placement.  The Vertex in this House can indicate a destined connection with animals and perhaps asks you to develop the ability to understand and, when needed, be of assistance to other species.
|The AntiVertex in the 12th House will give you a measure of psychic ability. As you develop your ability to be of effective service to others, this ability can become very strong. The test is to use it wisely and for the benefit of the community rather than just for personal gain. 

*Vertex in 7th House
Your doorway to higher awareness is through relationships. This can describe all forms of one-to-one relationships from soul mates through to business partners and even your deepest enemies.  You reach out to others and do not feel complete unless you can relate to them in some way. You search for your life partner and may have a destined relationship that changes your life. Sometimes battling an enemy opens the door to a profound understanding of your own nature and through that, the nature of those who originally seemed quite alien to you. Through relationships you learn about yourself and others and grow to understand that we are all part of the whole and all have a function in this world. As part of your growth of wisdom you may be drawn to be an advocate for another - the legal profession, counselling, speaking out for the oppressed or even a marriage celebrant are possible outlets for this need.  The area that is right for you becomes a vocation rather than just a job.
|The AntiVertex in the 1st House will require you to love and respect the body you have been given for this life experience and care well for your environment. You will learn that if you care for yourself others will love you. If you don't care for yourself others will tend to treat you with disrespect.

*Vertex in 8th House
Your doorway to higher awareness is through deep and often intense experiences. The 8th House covers areas in life that are usually quite profound - matters of life and death, the gamut of sexual experiences, surgery, research, and all recondite areas.  The nature and sometimes the compulsions of sexuality can be indicated by the Vertex in this House.  This placement can give experiences that run the gamut from forced sex to tantric sex and even celibacy, but whatever experience you have, it completely changes your perspective of the world.  As the Vertex axis is the doorway to other realities, the Vertex in the 8th House gives an interest in the process of dying and worlds beyond death. Many psychics who can talk to spirits have this placement. You may have a vocation to research deeper or hidden areas in life. Psychologists and psychiatrists who probe the depths of the human mind and emotions; scientists who research the atomic structures of our reality; surgeons who are enthralled by the structures and functions of the physical body and those who study occult and recondite subjects are four areas that spring to mind.  Alternative healing methods can be a passion for those with the Vertex in this  House as you realise that these areas offer a much greater understanding of the energy field of the body and the physical and emotional needs of living entities than allopathic medicine.
|The AntiVertex in the 2nd House will bring to you those with an affinity to nature or who are stable and secure. These people can help keep you stable whilst you have intense experiences or apply your mind to the deeper areas of life.  

*Vertex in 9th House
This placement can occur if you were born in the Tropics.  The 9th House is the House of exploration, whether physical, intellectual or spiritual. With the Vertex in this House you have a destiny to expand your horizons far beyond the culture into which you were born.  Contact with other cultures that are vastly different to your own can be the first step in this process, you may even find you are far more drawn to a foreign culture's religion or spiritual practices than those of your birth land. Your doorway to higher consciousness and to other realities can be opened through spiritual practises and techniques for developing your inner vision. The study of history and particularly the long cycles in history can be a source of enlightenment for you. You are particularly drawn to very ancient history and the cultures of those times as these can open doors to realities that are completely new and different to your own. Travel and adventure give opportunities for amazing experiences which open doors to new levels of understanding of yourself and your relationship with the environment.
|The AntiVertex in the 3rd House will draw people to you who are able to help you communicate your perception, experience and high levels of knowledge to the world. It gives you the ability to write and speak about your experience and therefore inspire others to seek their own truth.

*Vertex in 10th House
It is very rare to find the Vertex in the 10th House, but the AntiVertex here can take on this function. The Vertex in the 10th House gives a public life and a destiny connected to career and/or a destined career - something that you must do in this life. This destiny can come about in very strange ways at times. Your doorway to higher awareness comes through understanding management or government. On some level you will learn the needs of people and how to balance this with fair and just administration. You will develop an understanding of the different ways people think and feel and learn how to put the round peg in the round hole, the square peg in the square hole and how to liaise with both so neither feels left out.  You have a destined connection with a parent, who may be prominent in their field. This parent greatly influences you for good or ill and your relationship can affect a number of people who are involved in the same area. Your test is to be able to take the life given to you by this parent and turn it into something that delights and fulfils you.
|The AntiVertex in the 4th House will draw you to those who can give you a safe and secure home, a place where you can put your feet up, relax and be yourself. This is crucial to enable you to cope with the demands of a public life.

*Vertex in 11th House
The Vertex in the 11th House is highly unlikely. This placement will give a desire to benefit the community in some way. It will draw you to groups and causes that help humans, animals or even plants.  Your initiation into higher consciousness involves the willingness to develop a sense of the global community of all life forms on earth - and perhaps even in the solar system. This lifetime you are destined to meet someone who has a most powerful effect on you, someone who is a friend to you but also highly skilled or very wise in their field. You deeply respect this person and they act as a mentor who opens the door to new and different approaches to life.
|The AntiVertex in the 5th House will draw you to creative people whose skills help you express your ideals.

*Vertex in 12th House
This placement is highly unlikely. The doorway to higher consciousness is strongly stimulated with this placement and it can signify highly developed psychic abilities. You may find that you have very powerful, detailed dreams that can either foretell the future or give you insight into current problems. Your sensitivity enables you to know what others are feeling, both physically and emotionally, but at times you can get this mixed up with your own feelings and be unable to tell whether it is yourself or another. For this reason it is important to continuously clear your own energy field through spiritual practices and through the use of water - for example daily swims, baths or showers. If you wish, your imagination can be used to create beautiful films, stories and theatre as this Vertex placement gives excellent 'picture making' abilities. This can be the placement of a 'world server' - someone who has dedicated their life to the betterment of all creatures on earth. You may use the resources of institutions to help yourself and others. You have a destined connection to an aunt or uncle.
|The AntiVertex in the 6th House will draw you to practical people who help you manifest your compassion and ideals.

*PartofFortune in 1st House
Your greatest fortune comes when you show independence and self-sufficiency. A spiritual relationship with yourself and others will bring joy.

*PartofFortune in 2nd House
Your life is enriched through developing a set of values. Your lesson is to detach from others' values and build a firm set of your own spiritual values.

*PartofFortune in 3rd House
Your joy lies in communicating in relationships. You need to learn to think clearly and develop your higher mind for fulfillment.

*PartofFortune in 4th House
Your joy comes through being in touch with your inner self. Your greatest fulfillment is in the experience of new beginnings. You need to detach from worldly expectations.

*PartofFortune in 5th House
For you creativity equals joy. Your personal creations inspire beauty and joy. You need to develop impersonal friendships.

*PartofFortune in 6th House
Organisation and work enriches your daily life. For you, service equals joy. You need to avoid dwelling on a nebulous universal picture.

*BlackMoon in 1st House
If you are happy then everyone around you is happy. Conversely, when you are upset it follows that other people are also upset. You think that this is because of other people's behaviour, but you are the one who has an impact on those around you. Whether you realise it or not you have a dark side of your nature, in that you inadvertently lash out when you are upset. Occasionally this placement of the Black Moon in the 1st House of your Horoscope can indicate withdrawal from the company of others. Whether you withdraw or lash you, you blame others. You accuse others of doing wrong, and yet it is your unhappiness that is unsettling your colleagues or loved ones. Sometimes your own dark feelings can affect your physical or mental health. Once you claim your own feelings and break the cycle of blame, you are free of self-defeating behaviour. Self-understanding and acceptance bring relief, and perhaps joy into your life. You gain wisdom and may also choose to counsel others.

*BlackMoon in 2nd House
Problems arise in your life when it comes to money. You are likely to blame others for your money woes, but actually it is unlikely to be their fault. Your own self-defeating behaviour is, in some way, contributing to any short-fall in your income. The good news is that you can break the cycle once you acknowledge and discover the ways in which you are sabotaging your financial success. It is possible that your self-esteem is somehow linked to your monetary challenges. Perhaps you need to value your skills more and change jobs? Maybe you are procrastinating on a business deal? Or are you afraid of taking a financial risk? Perhaps you are too rash? Are you overspending, compensating for a lack of esteem and happiness? Whatever the scenario you are able to face the truths and create more financial freedom for yourself, and your loved ones.

*BlackMoon in 3rd House
How many times has saying what you think landed you in trouble in your life? Do you blame others? It is their fault because they don't understand, listen or care? Actually you might not realise it but your words can sometimes be harsh. Your darker feelings bubble to the surface and your loved ones can receive quite a tongue lashing. When they react then you blame them for their cruel words, not realising that you intitiated the argument. The truth hurts. If not careful you can indulge in all of the negative traits associated with this 3rd House of communication - whining, nagging, arguing, berating and criticising. Fortunately you have the ability to face the truth, to delve into the origins of the feelings that lead to you speaking out, and acknowledging the impact of your words on your loved ones. Once you have done this then you are wise beyond your years. You can lend a listening ear to other people's problems. Your understanding means that you may make an excellent counsellor or advocate.

*BlackMoon in 4th House
Whether you realise it or not you have a dark side of your nature, and you cause some upset for your family. You may believe that your family is the problem or that you have a right to express yourself, but the truth is that in some way you running away from your duties at home. You may expect family members to rescue you, soothing or solving your emotional problems. Deep down though you know that some aspect of your behaviour is upsetting your loved ones and needs to change. Even if your problem is something beyond your control you know that you need to stop lashing out at family members, expecting them to come to your rescue. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok.

*BlackMoon in 5th House
Whether you realise it or not you have a dark side of your nature in that you would rather play than take responsibility for your life. You can be a bit of a rabble-rouser. Your own creative pursuits are paramount, fulfillling a deep need within you. So much so that you feel that others, particularly children, are standing in your way. You may blame other people, perhaps even your own children, for preventing you from following your passionate interests. Nevertheless it is you who needs to find a balance between fun and duty. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. Once you have found this balance then you may be an excellent teacher, artist, and parent.

*BlackMoon in 6th House
The Black Moon is in the 6th House of your birth chart indicating that work can be a bit fraught at times. You may have trouble organising your diary and work schedule believing this to be the fault of others. You are given too many duties, your co-workers interupt your thoughts, the days are not long enough... Your list of complaints is endless. The problem lies within you rather than in others. You need to organise your own daily work-load ensuring that you assert your own rights. You have a right to say "no" if you are given too much work. You have a right to tell colleagues that you are busy to talk etc. You do not need to be a martyr. Nor do you need to overload yourself in an attempt to feel good about yourself. You need to value your contribution and take care of your own health and well-being each day. Others are not responsible. Once you have mastered these skills then you are a power to contend with at work. You may even choose a job associated with workers' rights.

*BlackMoon in 7th House
Whether you realise it or not you have a dark side of your nature, in that you are never satisfied when it comes to your major relationship. It is possible that you don't wish to marry because you can't find someone who measures up. Alternatively you may make a commitment, only to complain incessantly about your less-than-perfect mate. You find it difficult to be satisfied in a committed relationship, because all you see is the dark side of your spouse. The problem is that you are not seeing things clearly. It is likely that the intimacy demanded by marriage is triggering a subconscious memory of your parents' relationship. Whether you realise it or not an unsavoury aspect of your parents' union is playing on your subconscious mind. You seek perfection in your partner as a way of avoiding the emotional pain associated with old memories. Once you have acknowledged this reality then you start to break free and find a loving and rewarding bond.

*BlackMoon in 8th House
The Black Moon placed in the 8th House of your birth chart can reveal intimate details of your life that you would, perhaps, prefer stayed forgotten. This is because the darker aspects of the Black Moon are associated with sexuality, birth, death, debt, lust, greed and other such intimate matters.  It is possible that you attract, albeit inadvertently, the darker elements of society into your life. This can vary from the spouse who gambles irresponsibly to neighbourhood associates turning violent. You don't know why strange things happen to you, but they do. The challenge for you is to face the depths of your own dark side and hold it to the light. You need to delve beyond the norm, to discover the undercurrents at play. Rather than blame others for disrupting your peace of mind, thank them. They present your opportunity to face your own emotional, and psychic, depths.

*BlackMoon in 9th House
In affect you have a Goddess in the house of the Gods. This is not a comfortable placement indicating that you are at odds with society's establishment. You are likely to blame pillars of society for all of their faults - their rigid religious principles, unfair laws, infringement of civil rights etc. The truth is that you are rebellious. Your philosophies are quite different. If you have a reckless need to rebel then you are likely to cause strife, both for yourself and for those around you. However, if you can learn to agree to disagree with individuals, and society as a whole, then you can enjoy your unique approach. You may then be an excellent teacher, preacher, law-maker or philosopher.

*BlackMoon in 10th House
Whether you realise it or not you have a dark side of your nature, in that you are ambitious to the point of over-riding other people on your way to the top. It is likely that you don't see this side of your nature, believing rather that you are excellent at your job, better than most others. You have an air of superiority that can irk your colleagues, and you don't even realise it. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. Therefore you need to face the truth - your need to be the best is self-defeating. Others are just as capable. You need to learn to appreciate your colleague's skills and show them the respect that they deserve. This will, in turn, increase other people's respect for you.

*BlackMoon in 11th House
Friendships are a little fraught in your lifetime. You may feel that your friends fail to live up to your expectations, that you cannot count on them, or perhaps that they don't listen. The Black Moon is in the 11th House in your birth chart indicating that you like to be part of a group, to be connected to like-minded friends and to socialise. However, you often feel rejected and you believe that it is others who are rejecting you. In fact the opposite is likely to be true. You may not realise that you are quite fixed in your ideas, or that you are imposing your thoughts and feelings on others expecting them to agree with you. Any sign of disagreement is viewed as a lack of support. It is this and your inability to accept differences in your friends that triggers any social problems that you may encounter. Of course, you can join a group with similar ideals, but sooner or later individuals within this group are likely to hold different opinions and values. You need to learn to face your own intolerance. If you can learn to agree to disagree then you are likely to enjoy connections with other people from all walks of life. Your social life, and any work with groups, is more enjoyable when you learn to be flexible in your attitude.

*BlackMoon in 12th House

The story goes that Selene so loves her man that she cannot bear the thought of him dying. She uses her magic of the night to put him into a deep sleep forever. This way she may see him, unchanging, for all eternity. Can you see any strains of this myth running through your own relationships?
