The ocean is likely to fascinate you. Depending on other aspects of your birth chart you may either be a strong swimmer, delighting in the depths of the sea, or you may have a strong aversion. Either way oceanic themes keep cropping up in your life. This may also mean that you have a fascination for all things esoteric. You have hidden depths and may be a little reclusive at times, needing to withdraw deep within yourself in order to sort through your thoughts and feelings. You may even be a little narcissistic, resorting to feelings of victimization. You need to be aware of the affect that you have on other people when you are in this frame of mind. You may not be aware of the true manner in which you are presenting yourself and may need to turn down the volume on your complaints. Your lesson is to reach out to other people, see things from their point of view and realize the depths of your own strength.

*Sedna in 2nd House
You have deep feelings about money. Whether you are rich or poor, money holds a prominent place in your life, stirring deeps feelings that perhaps you don't even fully understand. All you know is that money continues to be a central theme. You may feel that the world, or someone, has been unjust and that you have suffered monetarily as a result. Perhaps your family was dirt poor when you were young. Now it seems that you are determined to redress the imbalance. It is also possible that you have had to take care of someone else financially and felt it to be a burden. Perhaps you made a large amount of money and invested unwisely. It is also possible that you benefit by victim like behaviour, crying poor so that other people give you money to help you feel better. Your lesson is to overcome your deep feelings about financial hardship and injustice, and to turn your attention to other values. What do you really value in life? What are your passions? An interesting exercise could be to sit by the ocean and ask yourself some deep and meaningful questions about money matters.

*Sedna in 3rd House
You are a very insightful individual, able to see to get to the heart of matters in any communication. The written and spoken words are powerful tools in your life. Your intuition is strong. You need to learn to trust your own insights, and to respect the hidden depths that you see in your neighbours, friends and siblings. You may, unwittingly, stir up hidden feelings in others. It is almost as if you have taken a big stick and put it into the ocean and stirred up lots of sand and mud. Other people may not be as capable as you of combining heart and mind. Therefore you need to use your powers for the good of others, biding your time and listening. You can sit very still and listen to other people's stories. This is a gift. You can also sit still by yourself. The ocean is likely to be a calming force in your life, helping you to focus on what is important. When you are feeling stressed, perhaps even depressed, you can go to the nearest beach to uplift your spirits. If you live faraway from the ocean you may benefit from pictures, or ocean creatures as ornaments. Playful seals may hold a special appeal.

*Sedna in 4th House
Do you live by the ocean? If not, why not? You can be deeply satisfied by living next to the large oceanic expanse, particularly drawing comfort from the sea life. If you do not, or have not, lived by the sea then perhaps you have traveled across a large expanse of ocean to live in another place? Family is a great source of joy, and perhaps pain. You have deep feelings, almost bottomless sometimes, in connection with your family. This can be either your childhood family, or the family that you form as an adult, or both. At times you may not realize the depth of your own feelings, and you do need to be careful of feeling like the victim within your own family. Of course it is possible that you grew up in a dysfunctional, perhaps even violent, family and that you were indeed the brunt of the negativity. This could have been connected to your father, or your father's family history. However, it is also possible that you simply felt lost in a sea of emotions and needed to escape to find your own sense of belonging. Your process of self-discovery is likely to be a rewarding one, as long as you don't become too introverted, living a cave-like existence. 

*Sedna in 5th House
Somewhere deep inside you is a longing to pursue an artistic talent or career. If you are lucky, and depending on other aspects of your birth chart, you can successfully immerse yourself in creative waters. If you are sacrificing your gifts in order to pursue a more practical path then you may become frustrated and ultimately sad and withdrawn. It is important that you dig deep and follow your dreams. Your talent is unlikely to be discovered within the four walls of your home. This placement of Sedna can also indicate a deep and abiding love for children, either your own or other people's. At some stage of your life you may cross a large expanse of water in order to create a better world for children, or to pursue your creative dreams. Listen to the longing of your own heart.

*Sedna in 6th House
This is a tricky placement of the tiny planetoid Sedna because it indicates that sometimes the demands of the everyday world get on top of you. In others words sometimes life's practicalities just seem all too difficult. As a result in your younger years you may feel a little lost when it comes to ordinary things such as, cleaning your room, doing your homework and making it to meals on time. As you mature small, but serious, tasks such as paying bills, putting out the garbage and servicing the car may never get done. The trick to this placement is find the meaning within everyday tasks. For instance the adage "cleanliness is next to Godliness" gives meaning to keeping clean and tidy. Other such adages may help. On a deeper level you could really benefit from meditation, prayer, regular exercise, a healthy diet and other such disciplines. For you rituals are relevant. You may also gain comfort from water pets such as fish or frogs, or small sea creatures. A daily walk by the ocean may be soothing. Once you have found meaning and pleasure in the little tasks then you are well able to handle the bigger ones.

*Sedna in 7th House
The simplest and most practical explanation of this placement of Sedna is that you need to find someone different, or someone connected with water as your marriage partner. You have a feminine planet in the area of your chart that is associated with marriage. Therefore your partner, whether male or female, needs to be an understanding and softer type of person. However, you should avoid anyone who appears to be bitter or acting like a perpetual victim. You need to feel a deep connection, one that crosses all boundaries. You may also travel across the water to meet your loved one, or they might travel to you. It is possible that your marriage involves some type of sacrifice, such as you living across the waters away from your own family so that you can marry your spouse. However, it can also mean that you feel deeply satisfied with your choice. 

*Sedna in 8th House
This can be a tricky placement for the tiny planetoid Sedna. The metaphysical 8th House of your birth chart already holds a lot of deep and meaningful treasures and Sedna is an expert at delving in. The problem is who is going to get you out of deep waters if you travel too far in? It is likely that you will have one of two paths, depending on the rest of your birth chart. One path is to avoid delving into esoteric matters at all. You doggedly refuse to admit that there may be a God, calling yourself an atheistic. You also refuse to merge with another human being in an intimate manner. This means that your sexuality is repressed, you do not share money well and you refuse to do business with another person. You can manage quite well by skimming over the surface, fearing the depths. On the other hand you could be the type of person to throw yourself in the deep end. You search the libraries, the Internet, the halls of learning and any resource you can find to discover the meaning of money, business, sex, relationships and the universe. You are diving for treasure and the more that you look, the more that you are likely to find it.

*Sedna in 9th House
You are a natural born philosopher with a deep understanding of esoteric matters. You are able to delve into any expansive subject and find the truth buried deep within. This is likely to be a profound spiritual or religious understanding, however; you may also be a learned scholar of law, science, politics, government policies and other such matters. You are likely to excel when you can immerse yourself in your studies. You may be the perennial student, enjoying the halls of learning far longer than any of your peers. As you grow in stature others turn to you for advice, and you may become a teacher, tutor or lecturer. You need to be wary that they don't shoot the messenger as you speak the truth. You may be tempted to be a martyr for your cause, being forced to withdraw from your chosen path because others don't like what you are telling them. You may even take a long journey across the waters to escape victimization. You are a zealot for digging up the truth, the crux of any matter. Do you realize how close you journey to the edge in your search for answers? Others may not appreciate your zeal, particularly if they are flouting the law. You need to learn to use your wits to protect yourself. This is not something that comes naturally to you, unless you have other strengths depicted in your birth chart.

*Sedna in 10th House
This placement of the tiny planetoid Sedna can indicate that your mother has played a vital role in your life. She may be a profound and wise influence, or she could be a deeply disturbing one. Either way her strengths and weaknesses have shaped the course of your life, perhaps even your chosen career. Even if you have deep hurts associated with your mother, or early life, you have the ability to delve into your feelings and use them for the good of others. Hence you may choose a career in the helping professions, or you may direct your energies into positive parenting. This placement of Sedna can also mean that you are prominent in your chosen field because of your integrity, your ability to problem solve and your insights. You are likely to be held in high regard by society.

*Sedna in 11th House
You sacrifice a lot for your friends, perhaps a little too much? Do you feel that you would go to the depths of the oceans for your friends? The positive side of this is that you are able to form deep and abiding friendships. You may even travel on ocean holidays with friends, share fun times at the beach or join a marine group. On the other hand you may be a martyr to the cause of friendship. If your sacrifices are too great then you are likely to end up feeling bitter when the favours are not returned. Your lesson is to gather appreciative loving friends and colleagues, while also making sure that you nurture yourself with quality activities. You are fortunate indeed in that you are likely to gather a group of loyal and abiding friends who stand by you for life.

*Sedna in 12th House
You are the ideal person to be around in a crisis. You are deeply caring and able to respond appropriately to situations that may overwhelm other people. You are sincere, understanding and well aware that everyone has a story of hardship, and hopefully triumph, to tell. You know what it is like to journey to the edge and be forced to rely on hidden resources. The problem is who is around when you are in trouble? If you are the strong and resourceful one, when do you get to sink? This is where you need to be very careful that you are not becoming a victim of abuse, or a martyr to other people's incessant need for help. It is important with this placement of Sedna that you learn to take time to recharge your batteries without sinking into reclusivity. For instance a holiday by the ocean, a spiritual retreat or a long walk in nature can be restorative. But spending endless days isolated can be too much. You need to learn to judge your own needs, when to help others and when to switch off. This way both you, and other people, really benefit from the hidden depths of your personality - the love, joy and appreciation of the universe.

*Eris in 1st House
You are a regular Tinkerbell or Peter Pan, a natural born mischief-maker. "Who me"? you ask bemused. Yes, you, although you may not be aware of the effect that you have on those around you, particularly those close to you.  You are probably a charming, lovely person, but you just seem to leave a small trail of emotional debris where ever you go. This is not necessarily a negative trait. In fact others can appreciate the way that you disrupt their lives, adding a frisson of excitement, perhaps shaking up a monotonous routine. No one is bored when you are around. You are a catalyst, the guest who livens things up at a dinner party, or any gathering. Your lesson is to listen to the still small voice within, the one that guides you to sprinkle a little positive magic rather than the one that stirs up mental images of mayhem. You can also put this trait to good use as a member or leader of a cause or group designed to change the status quo.

*Eris in 2nd House
Are your finances constantly in disarray? Do you battle to set or maintain a budget? Do gremlins seem to pop up whenever you try to sort out your personal finances? No matter how much money you earn, or attract, you don't seem to be able to settle down and enjoy your income. This could be because just as one bill is paid another crops up, or it could be because you are not satisfied with your lot in life. You are likely to have arguments with anyone who affects your income - your boss, wife, husband, children etc. This is because your lesson is to learn to stop worrying about every little coin. Of course you need to be sensible, but you also need to remain calm. Bless every amount earned no matter how small or big. Appreciate all the lovely gifts and possessions that come your way. Learn to love the things that people give to you, even those that do not carry a monetary value. It's magic. The gremlins then stop playing with your purse strings and you can enjoy a sense of abundance.

*Eris in 3rd House
Ah that tongue of yours can get you into real strife! It is not that you mean to say the wrong thing. Rather it feels like the words just rush from your brain to your mouth without a second thought. Not all of the time, but just enough to land you in hot water. Others do not appreciate your opinions, even if you are often right, or perhaps especially because you are often right. The problem is that sometimes you are not accurate. You have not listened carefully, or perhaps you have not respected differences of attitudes or opinions. Either way, your lesson is to listen, learn and carefully state your case. Often it is not what you are saying, but rather the way that you are saying it. Temper your thoughts, and your words, with love and compassion. This way Eris, the goddess of discord, will not run havoc when you are communicating. Others will then really appreciate the way that you think outside the square. They will listen to your bright and unusual solutions to problems, and be grateful for your insights into most matters.

*Eris in 4th House
Eris the Goddess of discord is affecting your home and family. This might simply mean that you rarely seem to have a quiet family dinner at home. You may even a large, noisy family, which is always on the go. Life is rarely quiet at home. Even if you are single and living on your own, you may prefer to eat out rather than settle in for a quiet night. Your home life is hectic. You may move frequently, searching for a place to belong. You may enjoy an itinerant lifestyle, or a busy home life. If you don't then eventually you need to face a few home truths. Why can't you find a place of peace within yourself? Is something troubling you? You may have to settle an emotional account with your father, or someone significant in your early life. Alternatively if you feel that you are at peace with your past and your own feelings, then you may have to make different choices that lead to a more peaceful or simple lifestyle. 

*Eris in 5th House
You enjoy competition. Not necessarily in sports, but generally you like to test your skills in one or more areas of your life. This can cause you some strife because others may be prepared for a co-operative and creative venture while you are all set for a contest. You may also have a tendency to opt out of any game, or pastime, that does not meet your expectations. You like to win. Have you ever been accused of being a bad sport or a sore loser? On a more positive note you can enjoy spectator sports, card games that test your skills and any creative enterprise that requires initiative, drama or aggression. If you have children, or work with children, then you may encounter some trouble as they grow up, particularly if you subconsciously compete with them. Positively speaking you may enjoy teaching a form of sports, or working with troubled children. 

*Eris in 6th House
The troublemaker Eris is affecting your daily life. This means that on a daily basis you are likely to experience annoyances. These can vary from unwelcome interruptions, to more serious problems with pets and co-workers. You need to avoid irritable workmates, grumpy bosses and unstable animals. You are not necessarily doing anything consciously to upset others. It is simply that you seem to attract problems. You can turn this placement into a positive one by choosing to work in an area that demands skills in fixing problems, soothing troubled animals, saving at risk people or animals or any job that deals with calming strife. In the meantime you need to do everything that you can to stay out of trouble.

*Eris in 7th House
Have you ever heard of the slang expression "trouble and strife",  a Cockney saying meaning "wife"? Well this is a most apt saying for you. Your relationship with your spouse, wife or husband, is likely to be feisty at times. Depending on other aspects your chart you may enjoy the thrust and parry of discussions, arguments and exchanges of opinions. You are likely to develop the powers of diplomacy through first hand experience. You learn within the arena of your marriage to develop a thick skin and to stand up for yourself. You need to make sure that you commit to someone who also enjoys competition, rather than co-operation, in your union. Otherwise you may alienate your beloved through too many clashes of opinion, and other aggressive behaviour. You may enjoy competition but your partner also needs to find this stimulating rather than irritating. Occasionally this placement can indicate someone who thinks commitment is just too much trouble, preferring a series of partners or living on their own to becoming seriously involved.

*Eris in 8th House
Money, sex and religion can get you into trouble. So you are well advised to show some restraint in these areas. You may already know this, steering clear of such subjects. You also need to think twice before dabbling in any of the dark arts, or the underbelly of society. The business world can also be a bit of a minefield, but not necessarily a deterrent. In fact you may enjoy the cut and thrust nature of business, money markets and other such areas. You are a born survivor, although you can tend to leave a wake of destruction in your path. You may make an impressive counselor, as you are not afraid to tackle sticky issues. You may also have a sixth sense when it comes to trouble, using this in your personal life, or as a troubleshooter in your work.

*Eris in 9th House
You have strong opinions on most worldly matters and you are not afraid to voice them. This is one of the more fortunate positions for the troublesome Eris because your opinions are likely to be debated rather than cause hurt feelings. In fact you may enjoy joining a debating team, lecturing or tutoring in a subject that you are passionate about or taking on the role of preacher. You may travel to avoid personal or societal conflict. You are likely to be well versed in world conflict, understanding the triggers for war and perhaps taking a role in reporting on world events, studying law, or working in a diplomatic field. You need to ensure that you keep a positive, rather than pessimistic outlook on matters. If you take a course in higher education, you need to choose carefully. Otherwise you might be forced to change courses midstream. Take care not to travel to troubled areas. You may prefer to visit historical war sites, or take a seat in a famous dramatic production.

*Eris in 10th House
You need to choose a career that helps troubled people, involves conflict resolution, or troubleshooting of some description. Otherwise you may find yourself embroiled in politics at work and in your marriage. This is because the troublesome Eris is in the career and marriage sector of your birth chart. You attract trouble with a capital "T" in your profession. You are likely to land in hot water at least once in your career lifetime. The best way to avoid this is to face it head on. Why not work with it rather than against it? Therefore teaching troubled children, working as a counselor or psychologist, negotiating Trade Union deals and other such professions could be just the ticket. In some cases this placement can indicate a disturbed mother, or a difficult relationship with your mother. However, this can prompt you to study or work in an area related to your experiences. 

*Eris in 11th House
You attract the lost souls of the world. You don't mean to but somehow your friends all seem to have a sad story to tell. You probably don't realize just how susceptiable you are to stepping into the troubled waters of your friend's lives. This can be a wonderful quality, however; you also need to make sure that you can enjoy good times with your associates, rather than just the difficult ones. You also need to be wary when it comes to groups, clubs and organizations. In some ways you are better off leading a maverick life when it comes to these types of collaborations. You are too competitive and direct to be very useful in a committee-style setting. If you do join a group then you would be better advised to run for Chairman, Director or President rather than one of the committee. If you are required to work in a team then you need to be allocated specific tasks to achieve rather than joint projects. You are likely to be a fine leader, soothing over trouble waters and sorting out any conflicts that arise. However, you are less likely to succeed as one of the team members. You may join a group that fights on behalf on other people, or that is involved in helping the world to become a better place.

*Eris in 12th House
You like to keep conflict deeply buried, rather than out in the open. In fact you may live in a fantasy world, not realizing the depths of other people's feelings until they seemingly erupt from nowhere. You are not deliberately ignoring the problems, you are genuinely not aware of the trouble that surrounds you, or the matters that your loved ones are trying to communicate. This can be a wonderful trait helping you to concentrate on demanding projects, meditate and pray for long periods of time and generally contemplate the finer things in life. You are not easily distracted, which is quite an advantage in some situations. However, it can also be hurtful to yourself and your loved ones when you are genuinely unaware of the impact of your own behaviour on other people, and their problems' effects on you. So what to do? Take a deep breath and learn to be very still - not lost in your own thoughts, but becoming watchful of the true nature of those surrounding you. You may also choose to work in a healing or teaching institution at some stage in your life. Sound can be very soothing ranging from the sounds of nature through to complex musical compositions.

*Moon in Aries
You have an emotional need for action and independence. Under stress you will seek a challenge and time on your own, away from other people. You may have experienced your mother as independent and possibly impatient. As an adult you are a go-getter.

*Moon in Taurus
The Moon is exalted in the Sign of Taurus indicating that generally speaking you are able to meet your own emotional needs, or find others who help you. You have an emotional need for stability and steady routines and like to maintain these as much as possible in your life. You may fear change, preferring the safety of the known rather than the unknown. Emotional duress can lead to you indulging in overeating, retreat from the world and perhaps even sins of the flesh. However there is an underlying practicality in your nature which helps you overcome bad habits and find a way of dealing with the world. Although practical you may also be creative and hence find release through massage therapy, interior decorating, cooking, the arts and music.

*Moon in Gemini
You have a basic need for mental stimulation. You are curious and seek answers to many questions. You are a chatterbox. When young, you may have called upon your mother to provide stimulation and activity.

*Moon in Cancer
You need nurturing. Under stress you may want to retire to the comfort of your home. You will form a strong bond with your mother. You may have difficulty in breaking away from home later in life.

*Moon in Leo
With the Moon in the sign of Leo you love to be the centre of attention. It's not necessarily that you like to be on stage in front of lots of people, but that you like to take centre stage in the lives of your loved ones. You want to play, and know all the tricks of the trade when it comes to getting others to join you. This can make you delightful company. When life gets tough you like to play in order to lighten up the situation. Parties, festivals, picnics and other fun events are the food of life, as far as you're concerned. 

*Moon in Virgo
You will experience a strong link between the emotions and the body. You have a need for perfection. You may become ill when under stress. Your mother may be critical or a perfectionist. She will provide you with structure and order.

*Moon in Libra
You have a need for harmony and peaceful surroundings, and will seek peace when under stress. Your mother may be social and harmonious.

*Moon in Scorpio
You have an emotional intensity, and a strong need for drama. Under stress you will create drama and intensity in your life. You may have been born at a time when your mother experienced a crisis, or your birth may have been traumatic. Your mother may have been possessive and intense.

*Moon in Sagittarius
You have an emotional need for adventure and independence, and an instinctual urge for travel and exploring. Under stress you will want to go on an adventure. Your mother may be seen as fun-loving and independent.

*Moon in Capricorn
You feel secure when life is structured, or you are working hard. You may be emotionally distant or cold. You mother's love may be limited in some way. Your mother may have been strict or cold.

*Moon in Aquarius
You feel secure with intellect rather than emotions. You may be aloof from emotions, or distrust emotions as irrational and unpredictable. You may have viewed your mother as emotionally erratic.

*Moon in Pisces
Your feel emotions deeply. You may seek reclusion when under stress. You have a strong empathy with your mother, and need to learn your own emotional boundaries.

*Sun in Aries
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Aries indicating that you're an assertive and freedom-loving individual, with a strong need for independence. Others may call you headstrong, but you simply believe that everyone has a right to assert themselves in any situation. Life presents many challenges which you enjoy meeting head-on regardless of the obstacles along the way. You're a natural-born leader.  The ability to focus on one's own goals to the exclusion of others is a healthy trait, but like all things a balance is needed, and you must make sure that you take the time to include others' points of views and modus operandi. On the whole though you handle yourself with aplomb as, astrologically speaking, the Sun is exalted in Aries emphasising the strengths rather than the weaknesses. 

*Sun in Taurus
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Taurus indicating that you're a reliable and solid individual, with a strong need for stability, routine and security. You approach life in a methodical manner preferring the tried and true pathways of familiar territory. In fact the adventures of unexplored territories fill you with feelings of foreboding and you can be quite stubborn in your refusal to leave your secure surroundings. Much of your energy is spent on making your world secure. For this reason you're appreciated for your reliability and ability to provide a safe haven for others. Tradition appeals to you, and therefore you're often seen as a stalwart in society, taking on the more conventional roles. Your down-to-earth nature also means that you literally enjoy the fruits of the earth. You also enjoy the sensation of textures and tastes, often indulging yourself in the comforts and delights of the sensual side of life.

*Sun in Gemini
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Gemini indicating that you're curious, lively, versatile and talkative, with a need for constant stimulation. You're adept at keeping your finger on the pulse of several things at once, like a juggler. Many times you weave your way successfully and skilfully through your many activities leaving others in somewhat breathless awe of your abilities. However, there are also many times when everything comes tumbling down around you and you're left to pick up the pieces which have been scattered throughout your life. Communication is a key element in your life, taking the form of lively conversation, letter
|writing, study, numerous telephone calls or even travelling to various destinations to satisfy your curiosity. You've a tendency to liven up even the quietest environment, sometimes even introducing a chaotic element. Life is never dull around you.
|

*Sun in Cancer
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Cancer indicating that you're a caring and nurturing individual with a strong need for family and comfort. Like the crab you may appear to have a tough outer shell but you're vulnerable underneath and will withdraw into your shell and home if feeling threatened. This withdrawal can happen quite often as you've strong
|emotional reactions. These strong emotions can be directed positively into caring for and protecting others, particularly your family and loved ones. When you're feeling an emotional equilibrium you enjoy giving to others, sharing warm and loving moments, and also enjoy your own company. In particular though you yearn to look after those you love, nursing them through illness, cooking a favourite meal or curling up in front of a fireside alongside them with a good book. You've strong home-making urges, and your home will be a great source of comfort to your friends and family. 

*Sun in Leo
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Leo indicating that you're good-hearted, and have a sunny personality which shines in the company of others. In fact you love an audience, basking in the attention which comes with being centre stage. Most of the time you do manage to attract the attention that you so keenly seek, as your enthusiasm and sense of fun has a contagious effect lighting a spark of fun and joy in those around you. Your generous nature also means that you're willing to share your abundant goodwill with others. You may also find yourself surrounded by children ready to join your playful games, for you're adept at bringing out the child in everyone.. Astrologically the Sun is said to be in its own Rulership in the sign of Leo, emphasising the positive sunny aspects of this placement.

*Sun in Virgo
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Virgo indicating that you're an analytical person with a keen mind, and will enjoy paying attention to detail. In fact you enjoy anything which requires close analysis ranging from pastimes such as mind-bending puzzles to more demanding work such as cataloguing data and scientific research. You excel in areas that demand
|concentration, organisation and rational thought. You love order, particularly in your daily life. This can include anything from an organised household to a properly-planned social calendar. Your loved ones will often rely on your organisational abilities, and these qualities may extend into your working life where others will come to appreciate your executive
|abilities.

*Sun in Libra
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Libra indicating that you strive to live a life of peace and harmony. This need for balance can be seen in all areas of your life, but particularly in personal relationships which play such a strong part in your life. Justice and fairness in interpersonal relationships are all-important. You can always see both sides of the story and therefore often find yourself in a peace-making or mediating role. You're diplomatic, and therefore carry out these roles well. However, make sure that you don't lose sight of your own objectives in your efforts to help
|others feel at ease. There can be a tendency to become so embroiled in the problems of others and in your efforts to make others feel at peace, that you forget about yourself. Artistic appreciation, and perhaps artistic talents, will feature in your life.

*Sun in Scorpio
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Scorpio indicating that you're a passionate and intense individual, who likes to experience life at a very deep level. None of the superficial skating over life's surface for you. You like to penetrate life's mysteries and the intricacies of personal
|relationships. You demand an intimacy and honesty in your life that can be challenging to others. In fact you're an excellent counsellor as you're insightful and not frightened of tackling the minefield of emotions which surround subjects such as death, sexuality and metaphysical experiences. You're also resourceful, in particular in financial matters. You often know the right place to search for information, or the right person to approach.

*Sun in Sagittarius
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Sagittarius indicating that you're a sunny and optimistic individual, with a love of adventure. In fact adventure plays a key role in your life, whether it be literally travelling around the globe, or metaphorically speaking exploring the world of ideas and philosophy. You're particularly enthusiastic about anything that expands your world
|and helps you forget about daily chores. Religion, law, sport, philosophy, academia, and ethics are just some of the many areas which provide a gourmet of ideas for exploration. For these reasons you're also likely to be attracted to people from foreign lands, who help to give you a fresh and different perspective on life. You also enjoy setting goals, as looking forward to a new vision provides excitement.

*Sun in Capricorn
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Capricorn indicating that you're a serious and responsible individual with a strong awareness of the 'right way of doing things'. You've the ability to work steadily and honestly towards achieving your ambitions in life. Others grow to respect your reliable and steadfast personality, particularly as you grow older. In fact, the people in your life come to rely on your ability to be a remain calm and detached in times of crisis. Mostly, you enjoy this role, perhaps even unconsciously adopting a superior attitude to those less calm and sedate individuals. You're ambitious, and enjoy working long hours to methodically and patiently achieve your objectives, as long as you consider the goal worthy of attention. *Sun in Aquarius
Your Sun is in the zodiac sign of Aquarius indicating that you're unconventional, friendly, unpredictable and innovative. Anything new and original will appeal, particularly if it goes against convention. You like to test ideas that have never been thought of before. Not that you will mind, for you're a strong believer in people having the freedom of individual expression and not being oppressed by society's expectations. |walks of life. In fact you prefer to mingle with groups of people, often adopting the adage 'the more the merrier'. You may also enjoy working in a group which fights a particular cause.

*Sun in Pisces

|and it is indeed important for you to find a channel for all of your creative energies, otherwise you find yourself slipping into a world of unreality and apathy. |side of life.

*NorthNode in Aries
This is a quest to become assertive and self-empowered. You have a tendency to be indecisive, always considering the needs of others first. Now you need to discover a sense of your own identity and initiate your own projects.

*NorthNode in Taurus

These attributes plagued you in this life because of suffering and traumatic endings in past-lives which left you with deep emotional wounds and a feeling of being cheated. In learning this life's lesson of trusting the process of change you will develop a newfound sense of peace and stability.

*Ascendant in Aries
The sign of Aries is considered "masculine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're more likely to actively seek your purpose in life, taking the initiative rather than waiting until circumstances are comfortable. Aries is also a Cardinal sign denoting enterprise, enthusiasm, self-assertion and initiative. You're frank, pioneering, headstrong and self-reliant. You like to be first. You value challenges, particularly those that test you physically and mentally. Your challenge is to see your ideas through to completion in any project, either by yourself or by ensuring that others can carry out your ideas. You also need to restrain your impulsive nature at times, to make sure that you're not risking your own and other people's safety.

*Ascendant in Taurus
The sign of Taurus is considered "feminine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're more likely to wait until you feel comfortable before pursuing your purpose. You're also likely to depend on other people to take the initiative. Taurus is also a Fixed sign denoting fixity of purpose, resolution, self-reliance and independence. Structure, stability and reliability are the cornerstones of your life. Your primary motivation is for security, in particular material security, and you aim to achieve this security through practical feats. It's likely to be a slow process towards successfully achieving your purpose, because you'll not be hurried. In fact you need to be wary of becoming too fixed in your comfort zone. The positive side of this tendency is that when you do commit to a course of action, then you can be relied on to come up with the goods.

*Ascendant in Gemini
The sign of Gemini is considered to be "masculine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're more likely to actively seek your purpose in life, taking the initiative rather than waiting until circumstances are comfortable. Gemini is also a Mutable sign denoting versatility, flexibility, adaptability, sensitivity, restlessness, indecision and anxiety. You're clever, cunning, intuitive and restless. Enjoying life at a fast pace you certainly live up to the Mutable side of the sign of Gemini. You delight in taking a flexible and adaptable approach to life, preferring to keep all of your options open rather than committing to one course of action. Your primary motivation is stimulation, because you hate to be bored. For this reason you're rarely settled in one place for long. You enjoy exchanging ideas with other people, whether it be through the spoken or written word.  Communication is vital, and you soon develop a strong desire for knowledge and expression to help you overcome the dualities in your life.

*Ascendant in Cancer
The sign of Cancer is considered "feminine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're not a risk-taker, but are more likely to wait until you feel comfortable before pursuing your purpose. You're also likely to depend on other people to take the initiative. Cancer is also a Cardinal sign denoting enterprise, enthusiasm, self-assertion and initiative. Caring for others is your major purpose in life. This could be caring for your own family and friends, extended family, pets, children or the elderly, or caring for humanity, or all of these. You're impressionable, tenacious, hospitable, sympathetic and moody. You've strong feelings, ranging from the most pure feelings of compassion to the most intense feelings of hatred. On the positive side your life is motivated by the highest form of feelings motivating you to care for other people, and bringing both you and the other parties a sense of warmth and emotional satisfaction. 

*Ascendant in Leo
The sign of Leo is considered to be "masculine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're more likely to actively seek your purpose in life, taking the initiative rather than waiting until circumstances are comfortable. Leo is also a fixed sign denoting fixity of purpose, resolution, self-reliance and independence. You're sincere, generous and ambitious, enjoying a sense of autonomy in all that you do. You're adept at organising your own life, and enjoy the independence. Generally speaking you're assured of your own purpose, and your life is full and eventful. However, there are times when your passion and haste lead to downfalls, and you also have to be wary of the dictum "pride before a fall". Fortunately you're usually back on track quickly thanks to your vital and sunny nature. 

*Ascendant in Virgo
The sign of Virgo is considered "feminine" by Ancient astrologers suggesting that you're not a risk-taker, but are more likely to wait until you feel comfortable before pursuing your purpose. You're also likely to depend on other people to take the initiative. Virgo is also a Mutable sign denoting versatility, flexibility, adaptability, sensitivity, restlessness, indecision and anxiety. You've a quiet, reserved, retiring and receptive side to your nature. Although you're not strongly ambitious you do persevere to accomplish your goals in life. You're economical, thrifty, hygienic, tidy in body and mind. Order and precision are your preferred modes of self-expression, and you like other people to follow your lead. Your intellectual ability could also feature strongly in your life, perhaps through research.

*Ascendant in Libra

*Vertex in Cancer
This will give you a magic touch with the public. You easily understand how to manipulate emotions and are highly responsive to the public mood. Unless other placements negate this, the public will instinctively love you and respond to whatever you offer. Your ability to feel the emotional flow in your world will continuously increase empathy. This can be a two edged sword as at times it can be quite painful to be aware of the sadder or darker emotions of human-kind. As a result you will need to periodically withdraw and become exceedingly private - you will want to completely shut the doors to the outer world. These private times can give you access to very deep insights that increase your compassion and wisdom.   If other parts of the natal chart concur, the Vertex in this Sign can give mediumship abilities. You have a connection to the sea, rivers and lakes that is deep and often magical - if King Arthur of the Round Table had been a real person he would have had the Vertex in Cancer! For this reason many of you love sailing in yachts or even in big ships. For some, fishing is a meditation that refreshes you - you don't really care if you catch anything.  Many people with this placement will find their destined home on an island or a boat as it gives both the privacy periodically required and close access to water. For good or ill family is closely connected to your destiny. Regardless as to whether you love or hate them their influence strongly affects your spiritual development.
|The  AntiVertex in Capricorn will draw you to those who can help you structure your feelings and present them to the public - writing, acting and healing are often chosen as appropriate venues. These people will also protect you when you feel vulnerable.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Cancer or the Moon strongly placed in their natal chart will be drawn to you. These people will comfort, nurture and protect you as you shed your old skin and venture into a stronger and wiser life.

*Vertex in Leo
Fame of some kind is yours. It is often thrust upon you quite unexpectedly and lasts for quite a while. It is important to embrace the fame rather than resist it as it is part of your destiny. The Vertex in Leo gives an ability to be noticed and loved that outshines any other - even the Ascendant or MC in Leo bows to this placement. People are drawn to you like a magnet and will happily do all they can to honour you and help you if needed. Love is your doorway to enlightenment and you can both give and receive love in abundance. For this reason it is wise to never abuse or neglect those who love you as this will diminish the power and beauty of the Vertex in this Sign. Part of your destiny is connected to children, either your own or those you are able to help in some way. Their innocence, energy and love of life stimulate you to greater heights of awareness and increase your own ability to shine. When you feel the joy of life you are intensely creative and often achieve fame through a creative area. If you find the joy of life is diminishing, then play with those who love life and this will replenish you.  As you have a strong sense of drama the theatre fascinates you and many of you find your destiny in this field.
|The  AntiVertex in Aquarius will draw you to those who have a strong social conscience. These people will open the door to areas where your shining skills can bring benefit to others.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Leo or the Sun strongly placed in their natal chart will lead you to areas of life that increase your capacity to love and stimulate your creativity.

*Vertex in Virgo
This placement gives you the feeling that you are destined to help and heal. You will not feel as though you fit into the world until you find just the right area. When you do you will develop tremendous gifts to offer those who need them.  Virgo is a Sign of magic - and particularly the magic of the Earth. Rituals that open a door to comprehending the powerful cycles of the Earth are part of the gift of this placement. Druids, followers of Wicca, those who are connected to 'goddess' energy and other 'earth' types of spirituality are often associated with this Vertex.  There can be a destiny connected to animals and some birds so it is important to always treat them with kindness and respect. This destiny can include plants, particularly plants that are of service to mankind in some way, so you may find you have a wonderful 'feel' for herbs, grains, flowers and flower remedies. Science or medicine can be a strong focus for this Sign and the Vertex here will at times give considerable inspiration in your speciality.
|The  AntiVertex in Pisces will draw you to those whose needs, compassion and spiritual insights motivate you to find practical answers and healing modalities to life's dilemmas. 
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Virgo or the planets Mercury or Ceres strongly placed in their natal chart will give you the help, knowledge or skills you need to help you make a transition to a new awareness of reality.

*Vertex in Libra
You dream of your soul mate and the Vertex in this Sign will often draw you to relationships that give you the feeling that you were destined to meet. These relationships can last for an hour or for many years, be happy or unhappy, but you never forget them because in some way they touched your soul.  Even a business partner or a working partner can open new doors for you. At times these people can be so different to you that you wonder why you are together, but they can offer you ways of seeing the world that you never dreamed existed. If you have a scientific bent, this placement can also be connected to artificial intelligence and even robotics. You can be fascinated by the various forms of flying -from space ships to parachuting - and particularly fascinated by the people who are skilled in these areas. 
|The  AntiVertex in Aries will draw to you those whose drive and vision motivate you to follow your dream.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Libra and/or the planet Venus strongly placed in their natal chart will entice you to meet new people and learn new ways of perceiving the world that completely change your understanding of life.

*Vertex in Scorpio
This is one of the most demanding placements in the Zodiac as the Sign Scorpio gives intense experiences and the Vertex axis intensifies this even further. Scorpio gives profound experiences in life and with the Vertex in this Sign these experiences will take you to its heights and depths. They can open your mind to amazing possibilities in the medical, research and scientific areas or show you the depths of human nature. Some of you will have sexual experiences that are so powerful they will open doors to feelings you had no idea existed and therefore change your whole life. The human singing voice can produce resonances that reverberate throughout your whole system and influences your moods and actions; therefore it is wise to make sure you choose voices that uplift you rather than those whose songs make you feel sad, depressed or angry. Scorpio is noted as the best healer of the Zodiac. With the Vertex here it is possible that you will have a destiny in physical, mental, emotional or spiritual areas of healing and become a powerful force in one of these fields.
|The  AntiVertex in Taurus will draw you to those whose stability and commonsense anchor you and who's steadying influence enables you to safely dive into the deeper areas of life.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Scorpio and/or the planets Mars or Pluto emphasised in their natal chart will demand you have the courage to tackle powerful issues that lead to a complete transformation.

*Vertex in Sagittarius
You are the most insatiable explorer in the whole Zodiac. Unless you have been traumatized as a child, travel and/or contact with those in other lands and faraway places are as necessary to you as breathing.  As the Vertex is the doorway to other realities, people with this placement can take travel up a notch. Many of you will astral travel at least once in your lifetime and quite a few regularly use this skill. Remote viewing is another form of exploration that you find enticing. You can't resist being able to psychically see people and places in the world that you can never physically visit. Proper training in this area is essential and fortunately for you, now readily available. You will find you are drawn to a country different to that of your birth. You have a destiny connected to a person born there, or the land itself and its cultures, past or present.  You may live in this country for many years or even make it your permanent residence. You may enjoy mental exploration as much as physical. You take great delight in exploring the great minds of the past; their thoughts open your own mind to quite different types of cultures and different modes of living. As a result you can develop considerable expertise connected to religions and/or philosophies. 
|The  AntiVertex in Gemini will draw you to those whose tales and stories stimulate your imagination and motivate you to further explore. These people will be able to help you record your adventures and insights as well as introduce you to people and places you find fascinating.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during times of crisis you will be drawn to those who have the Sign Sagittarius and/or the planet Jupiter strongly placed in their natal chart. These people will protect you and guide you through your difficulties.  Their abilities stimulate you to greater awareness and motivate you to develop skills in their area of expertise.

*Vertex in Capricorn
The symbol for Capricorn is the Goat with the tail of a fish. This symbol indicates that Capricorn has a spiritual and esoteric quality. As the Vertex is the doorway to other realities, it is very likely to access this quality when in this Sign. Capricorn builds the structures of civilisations, cultures, societies and organisations and your destiny is to be a part of this in some way. You will find that you are almost magically drawn to the people, places or situations where your skill can help build permanent foundations. At times you will find that information about an ancient culture can have a profound effect. You will want to learn all you can about this period of time and the information you glean can be applied to the present - often with a bit of a twist to fit modern ways. Crystals 'speak' to you. You have an instinctive understanding of their energy and how to apply it. You may become skilled with precious gems or have an extensive knowledge of how crystals can be used to align the energy centres of the body. Those more scientifically oriented develop an understanding of how to use crystals in useful way - for example, to power machinery. Capricorn is connected to the 'bones' of the Earth so at crucial times you can be drawn to rocks, minerals, mountains or caves for a mystical purpose. During these periods you will feel the need to withdraw from society for a while to re-energise. Proper physical alignment is important for you as this gives you the ability to access the mysteries of life and death.  You will benefit from an understanding of the chakras and the proper alignment of the spine and bones of the body. For this reason Hatha Yoga and spiritual forms of Yoga are of particular benefit to you.
|The  AntiVertex in Cancer will draw you to those who nurture and care for you as you put your full attention into your destined area of life. They will help you present your abilities to the public in an attractive and enticing way.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or at times of crisis you will meet people who have the Sign Capricorn or the planet Saturn strongly placed in their natal chart. These people will help you plan for the future and enable you to build new structures on the bones of the old.

*Vertex in Aquarius
Technology is just catching up to Aquarius, so for some the area of destiny has yet to be invented or has only just been invented. You have a strong social conscience and your destiny lies in areas that benefit people and/or the structures of society. You can freely give your time, expertise, inventions and even money if you feel this will benefit an individual, group or culture. You have the ability to see a situation from quite a different perspective and persuade others to see things in the same light.  Whether your choice of career is writing, music, science, invention, the social work areas or just ordinary day to day work, your input will always be original with a slant that brings new possibilities to that area.  You can have a profound influence on others. This Vertex brings a great interest in the mysteries of the universe that take you beyond ordinary life. Astrology, astronomy, science, physics , studying the very ancient past or using your imagination to project into the future are all possible venues for your quest for answers. Outer space, intelligent life on other planets and even the intelligence of other species on Earth are all areas of interest that if developed, can greatly contribute to human understanding. You can have a profound connection to birds which fly very high or fly very long distances. You may have an affinity with electricity and other forms of energy and, if you have scientific mind, may be involved in finding alternative forms of energy to power our planet, or on a smaller scale, your home or vehicle. Alternatively you may find you are drawn to the 'virtual reality' areas and your skilful imagination can find ways to make this seem very real.
|The  AntiVertex in Leo will draw you to those who have the flair and pizzazz to present your work to the world and motivate you to continue even when you feel discouraged.

*Vertex in Pisces
You have the ability to soar above the trees and see the whole forest. This is very useful in any area that requires imagination, inspiration or even technical expertise.  This is the Vertex of compassion. You are so aware of the gamut of human emotion and are developing comprehension of how this all fits together to create a whole. You lose the need to judge another as you can see behind the facade to their soul. These abilities can be used in many areas. Directing films is a talent that you may possess, even if it is only home movies. Music as an art that heals the soul resonates with you. As politics requires the ability to be able to serve large populations as well as attend to the needs of smaller groups with that population, it is very suited to this Vertex. You may prefer a quieter, more private life and if so this placement will draw you to meditation, spiritual contemplation and sometimes seclusion. You might find the life of a contemplative monk, nun or recluse appealing as it gives you the privacy to explore your inner being and develop wisdom. At times you need the wide open spaces - the night sky, the vast ocean, the wide desert - to give you a feeling of infinity. You wish to soar, to lose yourself in the universe, to blend with god and feel the ecstasy of this experience.  Psychic abilities interest you a great deal and you may develop those that require empathy, especially diagnostic skills developed through being able to determine where there is a problem by touching a person or object or feeling their energy field.

*BlackMoon in Aries
The Black Moon is in the fiery Sign of Aries indicating that you may not be aware of the impact of your behaviour on those around you. You may feel that others are overly asserting their rights and that you are not having a fair say. In fact it is probably the other way around. You are not realising the extent to which you are asserting yourself. You may be quite passive aggressive in getting your own way. Even as you read this you are likely to be denying the truth of this interpretation, ready to skip through. The planet Mars is said to rule the sign of Aries. Therefore you need to look at this planet in your Horoscope and claim your independence in a positive manner. Once you realise just how powerful you are, then you no longer feel the need to overcompensate by forcing your way. The BlackMoon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok.

*BlackMoon in Taurus
The Black Moon is in the earthbound sign of Taurus indicating that you may resist positive changes in your life through a stubborn refusal to move out of your comfort zone. Of course you may blame those closest to you, believing that they have not provided a viable way forward. However, it is actually your resistance that is proving the problem. In some cases there is never going to be enough money, satisfactory security or practical plans. You just have to take a risk. Once you have faced the fact that you are the one providing the obstacles then you may be able to take some practical steps towards achieving your goals, and helping support your loved ones. The positive Planet Venus rules the Sign of Taurus and therefore you are likely to be provided for sufficiently if you accept your limitations and don't impose them on others.

*BlackMoon in Gemini
The Black Moon is in the Air Sign of Gemini in your birth chart indicating that you have a real gift for communication, however; you don't always use it to the best of your ability. This is because you try to talk other people around to your way of thinking, rather than listening to their thoughts and opinions. You probably think that it is the other way around, that people in your vicinity fail to listen to you. You just don't realise how often you need to have the last word or how frustrating this can be to those closest to you. You need to learn to listen and respect other people's points of view and incorporate them into your modus operandi. At some stage you may learn the hard way, when someone actually walks away refusing to argue any longer. However, it is also possible that you persist in believing that this is their refusal to compromise, not your own. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. Therefore once you can listen and learn, you are likely to be a powerful negotiator. You can earn the respect of others and perhaps even excel in negotiating business deals, relationship mediation, and conflict resolution.

*BlackMoon in Cancer
The Black Moon Lilith is in the Water Sign of Cancer in your birth chart indicating that you have a tendency to be emotionally manipulative. You may think that it is your loved ones who are the moody ones, but this is not always the case. When you are upset you sulk, withdrawing your love and turning away from further communications. You are like your Horoscope symbol the crab in that you retreat. You believe that other people have withdrawn their love and approval, but you need to face the fact that you do not deal very well with your own hurt feelings. Your insecurities may be ruining your chances at loving relationships. Once you realise that you can change the way that you respond to your own and other people's feelings, then you are free to connect with others at a deep and fulfilling level. The Moon is said to rule the Sign of Cancer, which means that your needs can be met once you have faced a few home truths.

*BlackMoon in Leo
The Black Moon is in the fiery Sign of Leo in your birth chart indicating that you sometimes believe that other people are taking advantage of your good nature. You believe that you give, give, give and get little in return. In fact you might not be aware of just how much others are doing for you. In fact it is highly possible that you are the one who is taking, taking, taking and not acknowledging the support that you actually receive. The positive thing side of Leo is honesty. You know these traits exist and that you need to address them and you will do so. You need to acknowledge your need to shine, the support that others offer you and the gratitude that you truly feel. Once you have done this then you are able to give back. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. So you have the opportunity to achieve great things in co-operation with other people, either your loved ones close to home or co-workers in society.

*BlackMoon in Virgo
The Black Moon is in the precise and practical Earth Sign of Virgo indicating that you believe that you are always having to live up to other people's high standards. You feel that others demand perfection which means that you are doomed to fail. In fact it is you who sets the standards. Unwittingly you are pushing yourself too hard, and also driving those around you to live up to your expectations. It is a vicous circle. You are indeed destined to fail if you are always raising the bar, never fully appreciating your own and other people's gifts. Once you have realised that you are driven in certain areas of your life, then you can start to relax the rules. You are perceptive. So once you have acknowledged your own shortcomings, as a need for perfection is indeed a shortcoming, then you are able to see the light. You can lighten your own load, as well as other people's. You may even see the humour in such situations, and help others laugh with your gift for analysis and perception.

*BlackMoon in Libra
Do you have a propensity to procrastinate? Do you spend too much time gossiping rather than getting on with your own business? And do you get entangled in other people's business? If the answers to any of these questions are "yes" then this is likely to be the Black Moon influencing your birth chart. Your Black Moon is in the sign of Libra indicating that you are often focussed on other people's affairs rather than your own. An offshoot of this trait can be that you never have enough money. This is because of your lack of focus on your own business and the fact that you don't want to upset other people. You are a people-pleaser. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. Therefore you move forward rapidly on your own life's journey once you learn to assert yourself, and focus on matters at hand.

*BlackMoon in Scorpio
Do you feel that you are often embroiled in other people's emotional dramas? The Black Moon is in the intense Sign of Scorpio in your birth chart indicating that you often feel that other people invade your life with their crises. You sometimes crave solitude and resent their intrusion. Perhaps you don't realise the extent to which you are attracted to these dramas. You feel a little more alive and connected to other people when sharing intense moments. Therefore you need to accept your own need for emotional intensity. You may even decide to opt for work that demands intense concentration, or some form of counselling.

*BlackMoon in Sagittarius
You have a tendency to throw yourself into new ventures, determined to be exhilarated physically, emotionally or mentally. This can be a positive trait if you show some self-restraint and consider those around you. However, the Black Moon in the Sign of Sagittarius indicates that you are somewhat reckless in pursuit of your goals. Imagine a team of horses galloping out of control with a carriage bouncing around behind them. Ask some of the people close to you if they can perhaps identify with this imagery. Do they feel as if you are the team of horses and they are riding in an out-of-control carriage? You might be surprised by their answers. You don't fully realise how the exuberant side of your nature takes over. You don't mean to bully your loved ones and colleagues, but this can be the effect if you are not careful. This sensitive point represents the darker side of your nature, characteristics you know exist and need to address, but prefer not to acknowledge. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. Therefore once you recognise the need to temper your enthusiasm, and to give others the freedom to express their own passion, then you have the makings of an effective teacher or leader.

*BlackMoon in Capricorn
You like to be in charge. There is nothing wrong with this trait. In fact it means that you are often willing to take responsibility when others are not. However, the problem comes in that you don't recognise when the need to let go. You don't mean to impose your will on other people. At one level you may believe that you can do a better job, or perhaps you think that you are the only one available. You may not be conscious of excluding other people, but you do. Sooner or later those around you are likely to resent your need for control. The Black Moon represents the darker side of your nature, characteristics you know exist and need to address, but prefer not to acknowledge. This sensitive point is in the serious Sign of Capricorn in your birth chart. Hence your need to be in charge - of everything! You may think that others are trying to tell you what to do, but they are most likely simply trying to help you loosen up a little. You need to face the fact that your sense of duty is self-defeating. Once you can let go, and let others have a say and assist, then you are likely to feel much better. Your strength is accentuated as you learn to be more flexible.

*BlackMoon in Aquarius
Friendships are a little fraught in your lifetime. You may feel that your friends fail to live up to your expectations, that you cannot count on them, or perhaps that they don't listen. The Black Moon is in the Air Sign of Aquarius in your birth chart indicating that you like to be part of a group, to be connected to like-minded friends and to socialise. However, you often feel rejected and you believe that it is others who are rejecting you. In fact the opposite is likely to be true. You may not realise that you are quite fixed in your ideas, or that you are imposing your thoughts and feelings on others expecting them to agree with you. Any sign of disagreement is viewed as a lack of support. It is this and your inability to accept differences in your friends that triggers any social problems that you may encounter. Of course, you can join a group with similar ideals, but sooner or later individuals within this group are likely to hold different opinions and values. You need to learn to face your own intolerance. If you can learn to agree to disagree then you are likely to enjoy connections with other people from all walks of life. Your social life, and any work with groups, is more enjoyable when you learn to be flexible in your attitude.

*BlackMoon in Pisces
What a sensitive soul you are. The trouble with this placement of the Black Moon in the Sign of Pisces is that you don't fully accept the emotional side of your nature. You shy away from deep connections with other people believing that they are too unstable, or conversely not logical enough for you. What you may not realise is that you are not being rational. What you think is true of other people is actually true of you. Believe it or not you are the sensitive one, reacting through your feelings rather than applying reason. You need to accept this part of your nature so that you can then truly connect with other human beings. This sensitive point represents the darker side of your nature, characteristics you know exist and need to address, but prefer not to acknowledge. The Black Moon's gift is the opportunity to bring unconscious or self-defeating behaviour into the light of day where it can no longer run amok. So whenever you behave in a critical manner, stop. Think about it. Are you hurting someone else's feelings? Are your feelings hurt? Take a deep breath and plunge into the world of emotions. You may be surprised by the depth of your own feelings, and the rewards that come with letting go.
