As the Vertex is the doorway to other realities, it is very likely to access this quality when in this Sign. Capricorn builds the structures of civilisations, cultures, societies and organisations and your destiny is to be a part of this in some way. You will find that you are almost magically drawn to the people, places or situations where your skill can help build permanent foundations. At times you will find that information about an ancient culture can have a profound effect. You will want to learn all you can about this period of time and the information you glean can be applied to the present - often with a bit of a twist to fit modern ways. Crystals 'speak' to you. You have an instinctive understanding of their energy and how to apply it. You may become skilled with precious gems or have an extensive knowledge of how crystals can be used to align the energy centres of the body. Those more scientifically oriented develop an understanding of how to use crystals in useful way - for example, to power machinery. Capricorn is connected to the 'bones' of the Earth so at crucial times you can be drawn to rocks, minerals, mountains or caves for a mystical purpose. During these periods you will feel the need to withdraw from society for a while to re-energise. Proper physical alignment is important for you as this gives you the ability to access the mysteries of life and death.  You will benefit from an understanding of the chakras and the proper alignment of the spine and bones of the body. For this reason Hatha Yoga and spiritual forms of Yoga are of particular benefit to you.
|The  AntiVertex in Cancer will draw you to those who nurture and care for you as you put your full attention into your destined area of life. They will help you present your abilities to the public in an attractive and enticing way.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or at times of crisis you will meet people who have the Sign Capricorn or the planet Saturn strongly placed in their natal chart. These people will help you plan for the future and enable you to build new structures on the bones of the old.

*AntiVertex in Leo
Technology is just catching up to Aquarius, so for some the area of destiny has yet to be invented or has only just been invented. You have a strong social conscience and your destiny lies in areas that benefit people and/or the structures of society. You can freely give your time, expertise, inventions and even money if you feel this will benefit an individual, group or culture. You have the ability to see a situation from quite a different perspective and persuade others to see things in the same light.  Whether your choice of career is writing, music, science, invention, the social work areas or just ordinary day to day work, your input will always be original with a slant that brings new possibilities to that area.  You can have a profound influence on others. This Vertex brings a great interest in the mysteries of the universe that take you beyond ordinary life. Astrology, astronomy, science, physics , studying the very ancient past or using your imagination to project into the future are all possible venues for your quest for answers. Outer space, intelligent life on other planets and even the intelligence of other species on Earth are all areas of interest that if developed, can greatly contribute to human understanding. You can have a profound connection to birds which fly very high or fly very long distances. You may have an affinity with electricity and other forms of energy and, if you have scientific mind, may be involved in finding alternative forms of energy to power our planet, or on a smaller scale, your home or vehicle. Alternatively you may find you are drawn to the 'virtual reality' areas and your skilful imagination can find ways to make this seem very real.
|The  AntiVertex in Leo will draw you to those who have the flair and pizzazz to present your work to the world and motivate you to continue even when you feel discouraged. 
|At times of important changes in your life and/or at times of crisis you will meet people who have the Sign Aquarius and/or the planets Uranus or Saturn strongly placed in their natal chart. These people will be able to grasp your ideas and support you in your endeavours.

*AntiVertex in Virgo
You have the ability to soar above the trees and see the whole forest. This is very useful in any area that requires imagination, inspiration or even technical expertise.  This is the Vertex of compassion. You are so aware of the gamut of human emotion and are developing comprehension of how this all fits together to create a whole. You lose the need to judge another as you can see behind the facade to their soul. These abilities can be used in many areas. Directing films is a talent that you may possess, even if it is only home movies. Music as an art that heals the soul resonates with you. As politics requires the ability to be able to serve large populations as well as attend to the needs of smaller groups with that population, it is very suited to this Vertex. You may prefer a quieter, more private life and if so this placement will draw you to meditation, spiritual contemplation and sometimes seclusion. You might find the life of a contemplative monk, nun or recluse appealing as it gives you the privacy to explore your inner being and develop wisdom. At times you need the wide open spaces - the night sky, the vast ocean, the wide desert - to give you a feeling of infinity. You wish to soar, to lose yourself in the universe, to blend with god and feel the ecstasy of this experience.  Psychic abilities interest you a great deal and you may develop those that require empathy, especially diagnostic skills developed through being able to determine where there is a problem by touching a person or object or feeling their energy field.
|The  AntiVertex in Virgo will draw you to those whose practical mind and technical skills complement your abilities. These people are able to organise the tools and people you need to fulfil your purpose.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or at times of crisis you will meet people who have the Sign Pisces or the planets Neptune or Jupiter strongly placed in their natal chart. These people will give you the inspiration, compassion and understanding to motivate you to move into a higher level of universal awareness.

*AntiVertex in Libra
At times you have an almost compulsive need to open doors to entirely new worlds. You are by nature curious and desire to pioneer original concepts or new techniques in combat, sport, adventure and anything that requires a sense of discovery. You can be persuasive, dynamic and an excellent motivator for others who are interested in the same area. You will develop an intensity of focussed skill in your vocation. You can be extremely inventive and are often drawn to start something new, pioneer new ideas and develop new concepts - you just know that they will work and nothing can dissuade you.  Sometimes your ideas seem to come out of nowhere and yet are just right for the situation.
|The AntiVertex in Libra will draw those to you who help you communicate your vision.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Aries or the planet Mars strongly placed in their natal chart will lead you to areas of life that increase your capacity to love and stimulate your creativity.

*AntiVertex in Scorpio
You may have a deep love of nature and seek to develop an understanding of its cycles and mysteries. The plants and creatures of the earth will be your teachers as you open your mind to other realities.  You will gain much wisdom through learning about the magnetic fields and energy grids of our planet.  Your senses and sensual nature can lead you to higher awareness. Tantric sex can be a doorway to enlightenment; aromas can open your mind and senses to this world in a way that few others can understand. Sound of all kinds will enthral you. Music can fill you with delight and be a powerful catalyst to enable you to reach higher awareness. For some of you, money and finance is your vocation and you seem to have a magic touch in these areas.
|The AntiVertex in Scorpio will draw those to you who have intense insights into the deeper side of nature and/or whom have powerful abilities in music that compliment your own.  At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis, those who have the sign Taurus or the planet Venus prominent in their natal chart will be drawn to you to give you a different perspective and help take you to a new level of awareness.

*AntiVertex in Sagittarius
The Vertex in this Sign deepens and adds power and focus to all areas related to communication. It gives you skill and dexterity that you can use in most unusual ways.  You will be strongly drawn to an area that requires communicative ability and this can open your mind to worlds that fascinate you.  Writing, reporting, speaking, teaching, film and theatre are doorways to knowledge that changes your life. The focussed dexterity that this Vertex offers can draw you to magic, sleight of hand, music, dance or yoga.  These pursuits can give you the ability to lose yourself in the energies of the universe and return vitalised and refreshed. You may have a destiny connected to birds. It is important that you are always kind and loving to these creatures of the air. The ancient Celtic skill of being able to talk to birds and perhaps understand the messages of crows may be yours if you wish. In modern days this destiny often translates to aeroplanes, gliding and other types of machines connected to flying.
|The AntiVertex in Sagittarius will draw you to those whose explorative skills match your curiosity and whose information stimulates you to seek greater understanding of the mysteries of life.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the sign Gemini or the planet Mercury strongly placed in their natal chart will be drawn to you to help open the door to a new, wiser phase in your life.

*AntiVertex in Capricorn
This will give you a magic touch with the public. You easily understand how to manipulate emotions and are highly responsive to the public mood. Unless other placements negate this, the public will instinctively love you and respond to whatever you offer. Your ability to feel the emotional flow in your world will continuously increase empathy. This can be a two edged sword as at times it can be quite painful to be aware of the sadder or darker emotions of human-kind. As a result you will need to periodically withdraw and become exceedingly private - you will want to completely shut the doors to the outer world. These private times can give you access to very deep insights that increase your compassion and wisdom.   If other parts of the natal chart concur, the Vertex in this Sign can give mediumship abilities. You have a connection to the sea, rivers and lakes that is deep and often magical - if King Arthur of the Round Table had been a real person he would have had the Vertex in Cancer! For this reason many of you love sailing in yachts or even in big ships. For some, fishing is a meditation that refreshes you - you don't really care if you catch anything.  Many people with this placement will find their destined home on an island or a boat as it gives both the privacy periodically required and close access to water. For good or ill family is closely connected to your destiny. Regardless as to whether you love or hate them their influence strongly affects your spiritual development.
|The  AntiVertex in Capricorn will draw you to those who can help you structure your feelings and present them to the public - writing, acting and healing are often chosen as appropriate venues. These people will also protect you when you feel vulnerable.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Cancer or the Moon strongly placed in their natal chart will be drawn to you. These people will comfort, nurture and protect you as you shed your old skin and venture into a stronger and wiser life.

*AntiVertex in Aquarius
Fame of some kind is yours. It is often thrust upon you quite unexpectedly and lasts for quite a while. It is important to embrace the fame rather than resist it as it is part of your destiny. The Vertex in Leo gives an ability to be noticed and loved that outshines any other - even the Ascendant or MC in Leo bows to this placement. People are drawn to you like a magnet and will happily do all they can to honour you and help you if needed. Love is your doorway to enlightenment and you can both give and receive love in abundance. For this reason it is wise to never abuse or neglect those who love you as this will diminish the power and beauty of the Vertex in this Sign. Part of your destiny is connected to children, either your own or those you are able to help in some way. Their innocence, energy and love of life stimulate you to greater heights of awareness and increase your own ability to shine. When you feel the joy of life you are intensely creative and often achieve fame through a creative area. If you find the joy of life is diminishing, then play with those who love life and this will replenish you.  As you have a strong sense of drama the theatre fascinates you and many of you find your destiny in this field.
|The  AntiVertex in Aquarius will draw you to those who have a strong social conscience. These people will open the door to areas where your shining skills can bring benefit to others.
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Leo or the Sun strongly placed in their natal chart will lead you to areas of life that increase your capacity to love and stimulate your creativity.

*AntiVertex in Pisces
This placement gives you the feeling that you are destined to help and heal. You will not feel as though you fit into the world until you find just the right area. When you do you will develop tremendous gifts to offer those who need them.  Virgo is a Sign of magic - and particularly the magic of the Earth. Rituals that open a door to comprehending the powerful cycles of the Earth are part of the gift of this placement. Druids, followers of Wicca, those who are connected to 'goddess' energy and other 'earth' types of spirituality are often associated with this Vertex.  There can be a destiny connected to animals and some birds so it is important to always treat them with kindness and respect. This destiny can include plants, particularly plants that are of service to mankind in some way, so you may find you have a wonderful 'feel' for herbs, grains, flowers and flower remedies. Science or medicine can be a strong focus for this Sign and the Vertex here will at times give considerable inspiration in your speciality.
|The  AntiVertex in Pisces will draw you to those whose needs, compassion and spiritual insights motivate you to find practical answers and healing modalities to life's dilemmas. 
|At times of important changes in your life and/or during moments of crisis those who have the Sign Virgo or the planets Mercury or Ceres strongly placed in their natal chart will give you the help, knowledge or skills you need to help you make a transition to a new awareness of reality.

*WhiteMoon in Aries
You are a beacon in the dark for those around you, a real shepherd in charge of a flock. Whether you like it or not others look to you for your pioneering spirit. You can protect those who come into your fold. Equally you are able to strike out a path on which others can follow. You are destined to wash away your own sins during this life time, before moving towards your chosen path.

*WhiteMoon in Taurus
You are destined to walk away from earthly pleasures and treasures in favour of spiritual rewards. The delights of the five senses certainly hold their appeal, but you are interested in exploring a sixth sense. You may work with the earth's resources and help others to manifest their heart's desires. However, it is also possible that you shine a light on spiritual resources.

*WhiteMoon in Gemini
You are a natural when it comes to networks, particularly human networks. You understand the importance of communication. You have a love of language, and a good understanding of, or an innate talent for self-expression. Your voice and hands are instruments of your soul. You may choose to teach others, or to somehow lead them to better self-expression. You can be a real breath of fresh air.

*WhiteMoon in Cancer
The family is sacred as far as you are concerned. You may be well aware of the pitfalls of dysfunctional families, but you are well aware of the need for each human being to care for each other. You are likely to be a prominent caretaker of your own family, but you are also aware that God's family is what is ultimately important. Therefore you are likely to have links in your personal or professional to children, families, and animals. You are a natural nurturer with the wisdom to know when to step in and when to hold back. 

*WhiteMoon in Leo
You are a catalyst in people's lives, helping them in some way find their own creative path. Sometimes your own, and other's attitudes, are a little tainted by ego. It is difficult to let go of your earthly need for gratitude. Nevertheless you have a warm heart and it is your destiny to help others' heavy hearts. Your love of the fun, the arts and children is also part of your life's journey. Women with this placement have a strong mothering instinct.

*WhiteMoon in Virgo
The White Moon Goddess in this sign brings purity of the soul to matters of the mind. Nothing rational is an enigma, although emotions may well be. You are a vessel for logical thought. Engineering comes naturally to you. You are destined to help create order through analysis, research, fact-finding or computation. You may also write or teach in order to spread your influence. Purity of mind is important.  It is also possible that you understand the harmonics of mathematics and the music of the spheres. You are a code breaker. 

*WhiteMoon in Libra
You are very observant. You have a natural understanding of human interactions. A quick assessment of any social situation gives you an immediate sense of the interplay. You are also a quick and generally good judge of character. As such you are able to influence individuals and groups, using charm and compassion to ensure that others are comfortable and comforted. This is a powerful gift which put to good use can inspire the best in other people. Your destiny is therefore likely to be linked to a caring or creative field. You may also have an innate artistic talent that uplifts and inspires those around you.

*WhiteMoon in Scorpio
The Phoenix rising from the ashes is a powerful image because of your ability to triumph over adversity. You may not realize just how resourceful you are. Challenges met on your own personal journey can be turned into valuable lessons for all who come under your influence. It is likely that you have a strong influence on those who touch your life. You are resourceful, insightful and also well aware of the power of good and evil. Your spiritual journey is important and you like to remind others of its importance whenever possible.

*WhiteMoon in Sagittarius
You are on a spiritual journey in this lifetime, destined to strike a fiery path across the skies. You inspire others with your insights and actions. You are destined to help others reach for the skies, setting goals and achieving them. You may have to be careful of an inflated ego. You need to remind yourself that you are a mere mortal, and have compassion for yourself and those around you. Ironically the more humility and gratitude that you can muster the more that you are likely to be a respected teacher or leader.

*WhiteMoon in Capricorn
Integrity is a highlight of your life. You respect the laws of the land, as well as the spiritual laws. As such you live your life according to both laws. You are respectful and respected. You recognize the deity in the most simple tasks and beings, and work hard to live your own life in harmony. You are able to live frugally when necessary, and teach others to do so too. You are able to pay attention to small matters that concern people, while also building structures that endure.

*WhiteMoon in Aquarius
You are a constant source of surprise. As such you delight your companions and loved ones. You understand the need for each person to express his or her true nature without fear of judgment. Yet at the same time you are also well aware of the need for societal and spiritual frameworks. You are likely to spend much of your time talking with other people, planning social events, or working in a people-oriented profession. You are also likely to have a deep love for nature and the environment, perhaps even leading others to a greater understanding of the need to share the earth's resources.

*WhiteMoon in Pisces
Poetry, art, music, and drama are likely to play a prominent role in your life. You may even be destined to share your own talent for one or more of these arts. When you are in tune with your artistic side you can truly lift other people's spirits. Communing with nature and with God are also high on your priority list. You are well aware that your own, and other people's souls need nurturing. You are just the person to do so. You may also feel that you have a special role in helping the downtrodden or disadvantaged.

*Sedna in Aries
Sedna has joined the planetary panoply as the slowest moving planet-like object in our Solar System. It takes 10,500 years to work its way around the Sun. Most people currently alive today will have Sedna in either Aries or Taurus.  To give you an idea Sedna entered Aries in 1867 and will then enter Gemini in 2024. Therefore any interpretation of Sedna in the signs is likely to be nonsensical.

; Sign on House Cusp Interpretations

*Aries on 1st House Cusp
Life is best viewed as a challenge. Your expression is active, spontaneous and assertive, and you seek autonomy and freedom of expression. You need to learn patience and restraint.

*Aries on 2nd House Cusp
You value your freedom and independence. This is also reflected in the spontaneous manner in which you spend and acquire money and personal resources.

*Aries on 3rd House Cusp
You are a fast-talker. You are better at initiating ideas and communications, rather than following through.

*Aries on 4th House Cusp
You tend to be independent of your family and background, preferring to strike out on your own.

*Aries on 5th House Cusp
You love spontaneity and new games. You also enjoy new and creative projects, often initiating them yourself.

*Aries on 6th House Cusp
Your daily life is far from steady. You like to start the day early, free to set your own routine, rather than being tied to a stable routine.

*Aries on 7th House Cusp
You prefer to retain your independence when in a close relationship. You feel more comfortable with an active and freedom-loving partner. You could become aggressive if you feel caged in by your partner.

*Aries on 8th House Cusp
You are willing to initiate joint projects, as long as your autonomy is not threatened. You are likely to take the initiative in sexual relationships.

*Aries on 9th House Cusp
You prefer learning about life through raw experience, rather than in the halls of academia. However, any avenue of higher learning which challenges you will appeal.

*Aries on 10th House Cusp
You are ambitious with many bright ideas on how to further your career. You will demand autonomy and freedom in your chosen profession. You may be self-employed.

*Aries on 11th House Cusp
You are a leader, rather than one of the sheep when it comes to your friends and groups of people. You have your own visions and goals in life, and only those who give you freedom will remain true friends.

*Aries on 12th House Cusp
You fear being overwhelmed by other people's emotions, and losing your sense of self. You may find yourself fighting the battles of others, and you need time out to rejuvenate and renew your spiritual direction.

*Taurus on 1st House Cusp
Structure, stability and reliability will become the cornerstones of your life. Your mode of self-expression is sensual and practical. You need to balance stability with flexibility.

*Taurus on 2nd House Cusp
You take a practical approach to money, liking both the security and comfort it offers. You value reliability and sensuality.

*Taurus on 3rd House Cusp
You have a practical approach to communication. However, you may become stubborn if others attempt to force new ideas on you.

*Taurus on 4th House Cusp
You are a reliable and responsible family member. You value your home and family, particularly the family traditions. Your home may reflect your earthy and sensual nature.

*Taurus on 5th House Cusp
You enjoy the sensual pleasures in life - any pastimes that involves physical gratification. You may enjoy singing.

*Taurus on 6th House Cusp
Your daily life reflects your need for a practical routine. You are a stable and reliable co-worker.

; Point in Aspect to Point Interpretations

*Moon Conjunction Sun
This aspects indicates a New Moon at your birth. This life will include a new beginning in at least one area. How you see yourself and feel about yourself are one and this can make you self centred, sometimes even narrow minded. You can lack objectivity and perspective.

*Moon Conjunction Mercury
You are intuitive and imaginative. Your thoughts and speech are strongly linked with your emotions. You speak with feeling. You are able to sense other people's thoughts.

*Moon Conjunction Venus
You are calm and gentle and enjoy the company of close friends. You like to surround yourself with beauty. You are drawn to art, music, nature, and spiritual pursuits.

*Moon Conjunction Mars
You are an impulsive and emotional person, although perhaps not so sensitive to the feelings of others. You often act without thinking. You are a leader rather than a follower.

*Moon Conjunction Jupiter
You have a generous and expansive nature. You take an optimistic view on life, and few things seem too far-fetched. You enjoy adventure.

*Moon Conjunction Saturn
Although others may not realise it, you are painfully shy and lacking in self- confidence. This stems from a lack of warmth and affection from a parent-figure, probably mother, when you were a small child. As you grow older and work on your self-esteem you will build yourself a lasting maturity.

*Moon Conjunction Uranus
You are a resourceful, inventive and independent person. You enjoy the unconventional side of life and need excitement. You will show the wilful side of your nature if forced to conform.

*Moon Conjunction Neptune
You are a soft, imaginative and sensitive person. You may feel overwhelmed at times by your feelings and need to shut yourself off from the world.   You live in a fantasy world and have difficulty coping with reality.  You may have developed an unrealistic picture of your mother, and as a result have difficulty letting go either because you feel so at-one with her, or because you feel so disillusioned. You need to develop your artistic, spiritual and creative nature and avoid drugs and negative people. This way you will realise your true potential.

*Moon Conjunction Pluto
You are an intensely emotional person, prone to extreme highs and lows. You love drama and intensity. This can create problems if not channelled into a creative outlet.

*Moon Conjunction Chiron
You are a caring and empathetic person. You have suffered from rejection by a parent-figure, probably your mother, when only a young child. As an adult you have become adept at looking after your loved ones, sometimes at the expense of yourself. You need to nurture yourself.

*Moon Conjunction Vesta
Vesta is the Goddess associated with the sacred matters related to everyday functions. She depicts the rituals of work and wellbeing. This connection with Vesta and your Moon indicates that you instinctively crave ritual for your emotional well-being. You are a loyal person, who shows your love through your actions. You need to nurture yourself and others through healthy habits, good food and regular quality time.

*Moon Conjunction Pallas
The Olympian goddess Pallas Athena was a daughter of Zeus, born from her father's head after he had swallowed Metis. The Romans referred to her as Minerva. She is revered as representing the wisdom of reflection and strategy. When combined with the Moon in your chart she emphasises your instinctive need to retreat and formulate a plan before making any emotional leaps of faith. You are a born strategist. 

*Moon Conjunction Juno
Juno is the domestic Goddess of the Zodiac. When combining with your Moon she highlights your need for domestic warmth, harmony and nurturing. You are likely to nurture your loved ones through food, get-togethers and general conviviality. As one astrologer once said, "Juno is the Nigella Lawson of the Zodiac".  This placement of the Goddess Juno also suggests that emotional bonds with others are important to you. Equality is an attribute about which you feel strongly. This is true for your personal union, and also for humanity. Generally speaking this combination is a blessing enabling you to meet your emotional needs through your connections with others. Others relate to your empathetic nature.

*Moon Conjunction Ceres
The Roman goddess Ceres is also known as Olympian goddess, Demeter. She is the mother of Persephone. She is the Corn Goddess who personifies the agricultural cycle of fertility and harvest, as well as loss and renewal through her daughter Persephone. Therefore you are likely to have a close relationship with women and an affinity with nature and Mother Earth. You are a born nurturer longing to tend to the needs of others and happy as long as you and your loved ones are feeling ok. You understand the cycles of life, and the undercurrents of relations between women. It is possible that your home is one that is predominantly filled with women. On the other hand you may surround yourself with female co-workers, friends and relatives. You are happiest when you are intimately involved in the lives of others.

*Moon Conjunction NorthNode
Your feelings are your compass in life. Your intuition is strong and you are being urged to come to terms with this emotional and intuitional side of your nature. When young you may have difficulty expressing your emotions, particularly in groups of people. However, this is an area in which you grow until you can freely express your intuitional nature in a new way. The more that you follow your heart, and ensure that your feelings are true the greater good you perform for yourself and those around you.

*Moon Conjunction SouthNode
You are a sensitive person with a tendency to learn from experience rather through books. Experience teaches you to harness your emotions for the betterment of your own life's journey, and for those around you. However, you also have to let go of part hurts and grudges before you can truly move towards your destiny. This lifetime you have the opportunity to forgive and forget. As you do this you will see clear signposts as to how to move closer to your goals. Doors open. People appear. Opportunities arise. You need only have the courage to embrace them.

*Moon Conjunction Ascendant
Your emotions are a prominent part of your personality. You are sensitive and intuitive, and will find that others respond readily to your emotional nature. You will learn much about yourself through your feelings.  Your mother may be a major influence in your life.

*Moon Conjunction Midheaven
This is a prominent placement for the Moon indicating that you have a strong inclination to find your purpose in life and express it through your career or through parenthood. Your emotions are likely to affect your choice of career. Therefore you need to make sure that you strike out on your own journey rather than trying to please one or both of your parents. You also need to ensure that you like and respect anyone who holds authority in your chosen profession. Otherwise you may feel uncomfortable at work. You are likely to crave recognition for your achievements. This may come in the form of praise from your colleagues or bosses, or if you receive awards in your industry. You are sensitive about your role in public, and seek a sense of security from your chosen profession. The more that you feel that you are steering your life in the right direction the more happy you are likely to be in all areas. In the same way that you feel comforted when your career is stable, you may also comfort others through your chosen profession. Perhaps you enjoy looking after your workmates, listening to their troubles and bringing them little treats, or maybe your career is in a helping profession, or the hospitality industry. Your life choices may be strongly influenced from childhood through to adulthood by your mother, or another matriach in your family. 

*Moon Conjunction PartofFortune
Good fortune is likely to feature in your life, particularly in connection with women. When your self-esteem is strong and you are feeling stable then you can attract wealth, health and happiness, particularly through your relationships with women. However, if you are feeling upset, lost or lonely then you may be tempted to compromise your good fortune. You need to ensure that you remain at peace with your own emotions and all will be well.

*Moon Conjunction Imum Coeli
Most people are influenced by their home and family. However, you are particularly sensitive to the ebb and flow of family life. As a young child you enjoy spending time in your home, relating to those who share your household as well as extended family members. If you grow up in a warm and supportive family environment then you are likely to enjoy an equally happy household as an adult. If you suffer at the hands of your family then your journey may be rockier. At some stage you are likely to break away, determined to create a sense of security in your own home. You may start a family of your own with the view of developing a warm and safe household. Safety and security at home are vital factors for your health and happiness. You need a safe haven. Your home does not necessarily need to be a large mansion, but you do need to feel comfortable. You are likely to be a force to be reckoned with in your family life. Other family members may come and go, but you are the one likely to be a guiding hand and a comfort for family members. You may be the keeper of family memories with photographic displays, books, and stories to tell. The family history fascinates you, perhaps even compelling you to research and record facts and stories.

*Moon Square Sun
You feel an inner conflict between your nature and your emotional needs. Your parents may not have agreed on how to bring you up. The challenge is to trust your feelings and to be assertive. Find your own way in life, following neither Mother nor Father.

*Moon Square Mercury
You are indecisive, spending much time weighing up the pros and cons. This is because your feelings and thoughts are at odds. As you learn how to compromise you will develop understanding and an inner knowledge on how to act.

*Moon Square Venus
You have difficulty expressing your feelings in relationships. You feel you cannot relax and be yourself when with your loved ones. Once you have learnt to reveal your feelings in a loving manner you will develop an understanding of relationships.

*Moon Square Mars
You are quick-tempered and intolerant. Your impatience and irritability can mean periods of loneliness when others leave you alone. Once you have learnt self- control you will discover plenty of energy to be channelled into your activities.

*Moon Square Jupiter
You have a tendency to be apathetic and self-indulgent, preferring to ride on the camel's back as it is more fun. You need to learn self-discipline to achieve your goals.

*Moon Square Saturn
You suffer from feelings of discontent and insecurity. You work hard to cover up your inner lack of self-esteem. Once you have learnt to value yourself you will find your self-confidence growing.

*Moon Square Uranus
You are erratic and stubborn in your efforts to stand out from the crowd. Once you have learnt to view things from all aspects your intuitive and exciting nature will flourish.

*Moon Square Neptune
You are moody and prone to depression. You feel confused and caught  in a web of emotions.  Once you have learn to value the softer side of your nature you will direct your talents into creative pursuits.

*Moon Square Pluto
You are intense and emotional. You find yourself caught up in emotional dramas wondering how you will make your life quieter, or if you really want life to be quiet. The answer is to direct your need for intensity into creative pursuits.

*Moon Square Chiron
You are a suffering and wounded person. You feel that you are misunderstood, particularly by your own mother. Once you have learnt to rise above your pain, you will have the ability to understand and help others.

*Moon Square Vesta
Vesta is the Goddess associated with the sacred matters related to everyday functions. She depicts the rituals of work and wellbeing. When combined with your Moon in this manner it suggests that you have some difficulty reconciling your need for routine and your other emotional needs. You need to find a balance, seeking daily activities that provide emotional sustenance. This Goddess is calling on you to express your feelings through rituals, to calm your emotions through daily practices such as yoga and/or meditation and to treat your body as a temple.

*Moon Square Juno
Relationships with loved ones provide you with emotional sustenance. Therefore you are likely to be nurtured, and to nurture your loved ones through food, get-togethers and general conviviality. However, you need to ensure that your loved ones are on the same wave length. For instance do your loved ones know of your need for nurturing through shared sustenance? Are you giving more than you receive? As one astrologer once said, "Juno is the Nigella Lawson of the Zodiac".  This is because Juno is the domestic Goddess of the Zodiac. When combining with your Moon she highlights your need for domestic warmth, harmony and nurturing. You simply need to ensure that you are nurturing yourself as much as you are looking after others. 

*Moon Square Ceres
Relationships with women do not flow as easily as you would like in your life. Perhaps you feel that you are misunderstood by the women who are closest to you, or maybe you don't fully understand their emotions. As a result you are on a path of integrating your own emotions. This means that you need to nurture and accept the feminine aspects of your own nature. As a result your understanding of women grows and your sense of loss lessens.

*Moon Square Ascendant
Your emotions are a prominent part of your personality. You are sensitive and intuitive, if somewhat reactive at times. You are likely to find that others respond readily to your emotional nature if you can remain calm and assertive. You learn much about yourself through your feelings.

*Moon Square Midheaven
Your emotions are likely to affect your choice of career. Therefore you need to make sure that you strike out on your own journey rather than trying to please one or both of your parents. You also need to ensure that you like and respect anyone who holds authority in your chosen profession. Otherwise you may feel uncomfortable at work. You are likely to crave recognition for your achievements. This may come in the form of praise from your colleagues or bosses, or if you receive awards in your industry. You are sensitive about your role in public, and seek a sense of security from your chosen profession. The more that you feel that you are steering your life in the right direction the more happy you are likely to be in all areas. 

*Moon Square PartofFortune

However, if you are feeling upset, lost or lonely then you may be tempted to compromise your good fortune. You need to ensure that you remain at peace with your own emotions and all will be well.

*Moon Opposition Jupiter
You struggle with your tendency to be self-indulgent and attached to the comforts of life.  As a child your mother may have been over-indulgent, and you may have difficulty finding the motivation the leave the nest. As an adult you may be self- indulgent lacking the motivation to achieve your goals, or you may be extravagant and have unrealistic expectations. You may lack faith in yourself and put other people on a pedestal. You have trouble finding the middle road. The lesson is moderation.

*Moon Opposition Saturn

*Moon Opposition Uranus
Conflict arises in your life because you believe your emotions are crazy. *Moon Opposition Neptune

*Moon Trine Pallas
The Olympian goddess Pallas Athena was a daughter of Zeus, born from her father's head after he had swallowed Metis. The Romans referred to her as Minerva. She is revered as representing the wisdom of reflection and strategy. When combined with the Moon in your chart she emphasises your instinctive need to retreat and formulate a plan before making any emotional leaps of faith. You are a born strategist.

You are responsible, serious and reliable. You may have had a stricter father than the other children. Work and a career will be important to you. You have the self discipline to succeed.

*Sun Conjunction Uranus
You are a rebel but also a leader. You are innovative and original. Others may see you as arrogant, wilful and disruptive at times. Life will be full of surprises. Politics, science or computing appeal to you.

*Sun Conjunction Neptune
Fantasy plays a strong part in your life, either as a creative channel or as an escape. You are 'other worldly', possibly artistic or musical. You may be unclear of your own identity. Try to use your creativity rather than escaping through addictive behaviour.

*Sun Conjunction Pluto
You are intense, obsessive and have great personal power. You find it easy to rid yourself of the unwanted but may be intolerant of others less powerful. Transformation is the key factor in your life.

*Sun Conjunction Chiron
You are a sensitive and caring person. This may be as a result of an early childhood wound, either physical or emotional. At times you may hesitate to express yourself because you are so sensitive to other people's pain. You have a compassionate nature as you have the ability to understand other people's hurts, but you also need to take care of yourself.

*Sun Conjunction Vesta
Vesta is the Goddess associated with the sacred matters related to everyday functions. She depicts the rituals of work and wellbeing. This Goddess is combining with your Sun Sign to suggest that your own well being is of vital importance. You need to ensure that you maintain a healthy sense of self-esteem and look after your self. Daily rituals such as yoga, meditation and exercise are likely to be highly beneficial. 

*Sun Conjunction Juno
From a young age you have a certain "presence". As you mature you are likely to become the matriarch or patriarch in your circle of friends, or family. This is because the Goddess Juno is closely associated with your Sun Sign, emphasising any natural abilities that you have to relate to others. You are likely to express yourself best when in relationship with other people. Diplomacy and fairness are likely to be traits that you value. You are fair-minded, adept at putting others at their ease but certainly no push-over. You are likely to have a strong nurturing side to your nature and keen understanding of human nature. You deal equally well with men and women.

*Sun Conjunction Ceres
This can be a positive combination indicating that you are able to nurture both the masculine and feminine aspects of yourself and those around you. It is possible that a sense of loss during your childhood has contributed to your understanding of the need to be independent and resourceful as well as the need to empathise with others. However you may also be a well-balanced individual who enjoys the company of both men and women, and knows how to relate to others in a positive and nurturing manner. This combination can also indicate that you benefit from escaping the rigours of a material world for sojourns into nature. You can rejuvenate your spirit through communing with the natural world. Beauty, peace and love are important to you.

*Sun Conjunction NorthNode
It is time for you to leave behind your past inhibitions and truly express yourself in this life-time. You will find that events in life will force you to come to terms with your identity in order to express your fullest potential. You may feel that your private life, your family and home are demanding your full attention, but you do need to express yourself through your profession or a public group. You may have a message which needs to be heard by many people, not just your own family group.

*Sun Conjunction SouthNode
You may struggle at times to express your true potential, but you need to keep persisting. It is time for you to learn from any mistakes and really shine. You need to be the leading lady or man in your own life. You get plenty of chances to learn, grow and flourish. You just need to make sure that you are not dwelling in the past.

*Sun Conjunction Ascendant
You have a radiant personality, and a strong influence on other people, perhaps stronger than you realise. You like to shine in whatever you do, and this is your best path to self-discovery.

*Sun Conjunction Midheaven
This is a prominent placement of the Sun indicating that you are keen to make your mark on the world. You want to leave a legacy whether through your chosen profession, an official position in a group or club, or your children. You like to shine in the public eye. This could literally mean that you choose a career that propels you into the limelight such acting, singing, politics or teaching. However, it could simply mean that you are ambitious, keen to make it to the top in any field. Your reputation is important. This is a fortunate position of the Sun. Therefore you are likely to receive support enabling you to achieve your life ambitions. Others are happy to see you have your moment, or moments, in the sun. You need only set your goals, pace yourself and shine. As US General S Patton once said: "I do not fear failure. I only fear the 'slowing up' of the engine inside of me which is pounding, saying, 'Keep going, someone must be on top, why not you?'"

*Sun Conjunction PartofFortune
Your joy, happiness and success is associated with the true expression of your Sun Sign. You need to fully examine the Zodiac Sign of your Sun to fully understand where joy and happiness lie for you. You can truly shine when expressing your Sun Sign traits.

*Sun Conjunction Imum Coeli
Your identity is intricately linked with your family. As a young child your family, in particular your father, played a prominent role in influencing your personality, decisions, values and all facets of your life. Depending on other aspects of your birth chart this could have been a positive or negative experience. Either way you see yourself as part of a family system. Whereas friends and colleagues may have struck out on their own path early in life, you are more likely to have stayed close to home and hearth. Even if you moved out of the family home, it is likely that you stayed in the neighbourhood or in close touch with family members. Quite simply family is of utmost importance in your life. All that you achieve is likely to be as a direct result of the positive, and perhaps negative, influences of your experiences growing up in the family home. As an adult you are likely to find a home and start a family of your own, as this is more important to you than establishing a career, travelling, or other such public adventures. You may be a private person, preferring to gather a few close friends or family members in your own home. Even if you enjoy social and professional forays you are still likely to require a safe haven - your home. You are likely to shine at any family occasion, and may prefer to work from home or be the household manager. 

*Sun Square Moon
You feel an inner conflict between your nature and your emotional needs. Your parents may not have agreed on how to bring you up. The challenge is to trust your feelings and to be assertive. Find your own way in life, following neither Mother nor Father.

You have an overly optimistic and idealistic approach to life. You are prone to excessive behaviour and can be egotistical. Positively, you have the ability to reach your goals.

*Sun Square Saturn

*Sun Square Uranus

*Sun Square Neptune

*Sun Square Pluto
You are an explosive and unpredictable person who has trouble controlling your emotions. You are powerful and good at rising to challenges. You need to learn to compromise.

*Sun Square Chiron
You have difficulty shining in your life because of a childhood wound, perhaps connected with your father. You  lack confidence and feel lonely at times. Nevertheless this very wound is the source of great understanding, and gives you a unique strength to help yourself, and others. One of your life lessons is to learn to find the balance.

*Sun Square Ceres

You need to fully examine the Zodiac Sign and nature of your Sun to fully understand where joy and happiness lie for you. You can truly shine when expressing your Sun Sign traits but first you may have to overcome a few hurdles.

*Mercury Conjunction Moon
You are intuitive and imaginative. Your thoughts and speech are strongly linked with your emotions. You speak with feeling. You are able to sense other people's thoughts.

*Mercury Conjunction Sun
You are an effective communicator. You enjoy intellectual stimulation, and look for avenues through which to communicate your ideas. You tend to talk forcefully about yourself and your interests but are less interested in listening to others.

*Mercury Conjunction Venus
You express yourself in a loving manner. You enjoy talking with people, and they find you a warm and welcoming listener.

*Mercury Conjunction Mars
You are a forthright and powerful speaker. You enjoy a thought-provoking discussion.

*Mercury Conjunction Jupiter
You are talkative and have a thirst for knowledge. You have big ideas and plans. Education will feature largely in your life.

*Mercury Conjunction Saturn
You have a logical mind. As a child you were shy and unable to express your opinions. As an adult you will become a voice of authority.

*Mercury Conjunction Uranus
You have an incisive and ingenious mind. Your thoughts and speech are erratic and inventive. You enjoy progressive topics. Your opinions may be ahead of your time.

*Mercury Conjunction Neptune
You have an imaginative mind, although at times you speak in a vague fashion. You are sensitive to the thoughts and ideas of other people. You are creative.

*Mercury Conjunction Pluto
You have a probing mind. You avoid social chit-chat preferring deep and meaningful conversations. You are able to research topics of interest.

*Mercury Conjunction Chiron
Early childhood education or communication may have been a source of pain for you. Perhaps you grew up believing something was wrong with the way you communicated with others, or that you were not as intelligent as your peers. This is unlikely to be have been the truth, but rather that you learn through experience rather than by rote. You are empathetic, intuitive and sensitive. As an adult you are a good listener and understand the pain of other people. You may choose to be a counsellor, or teacher. On the other hand you may find that your friends, colleagues and family members open up and share their troubles and concerns, knowing you to be a warm and understanding companion.

*Mercury Conjunction Vesta
Vesta is the Goddess associated with a fire that never goes out. In your case it is combined with the intelligent planet Mercury indicating that you have an equiring mind. It is likely that you have a thirst for knowledge that is hard to quench. You may be drawn to the study of something sacred, such as mathematics, astrology, geometry or mythology.  Whatever your choice of topic, you are likely to excel because you have an intellectual spark that is equal to none. Your intellect is unique. 

*Mercury Conjunction Juno
The manner in which you communicate with other people is likely to have a stronger than usual influence on your major relationships. While others may say what they think without necessarily impacting their loved ones, the words that come from your mouth have a profound effect on your nearest and dearest. This can be a positive trait if you are sensitive and loving in your communications. However, any harsh words are likely to be amplified. You must be just, calm and caring when communicating with others. This can indicate a talent for hospitality, advocacy, counselling, diplomatic postings, writing cook books or other communications that are connected with nurturing people. 

*Mercury Conjunction NorthNode
You are being urged to develop your communication skills. Your destiny in this life may be linked to some form of teaching or communication. This may also be linked with groups.

*Mercury Conjunction SouthNode
Your communication skills are highly-developed, but you need to avoid your tendency for talk rather than action. You are being challenged to stop scattering your energy in all directions and put your communication skills to good use.

*Mercury Conjunction Ascendant
Communications will play a major role in your life. You are curious and enjoy discovering new ideas, which you will also want to share with other people.

*Mercury Conjunction Midheaven
You are happiest when you are learning new skills, which you can use in to get ahead in life. In other words you don't like to be bored when it comes to your main occupation. If you are bored then you are likely to want to change your job, escape on a trip, or perhaps distract yourself with spending money or a dalliance at work. You need to be stimulated. You may well be an intellect, maneuvering your path through the school system, into post-graduate studies and then into a career that makes full use of your mind. Writing, teaching, lecturing, research and politics are just a few that come to mind. On the other hand you may be a practical person who likes to use your hands, learning new skills as a tradesman. Another possibility is that you like to be on the move working as a taxi or truck driver, a courier or operating some sort of machinery. You may excel in sales and marketing where you can fully utilize your gift for chatting with customers and colleagues. Whatever your chosen career the key element is that it keeps you interested. As a child, and as an adult, you are likely to get into mischief if your main occupation is boring.  You need to live by your wits, maintain your interest in your work but you also need to learn a little self-discipline. You do well to remember the long-term benefits that sometimes accompany short-term discomfort. Then you are likely to excel in any chosen profession.

*Mercury Conjunction Imum Coeli
Ancient astrologers considered this placement to be a prominent one indicating that the planet Mercury, and all things related, are likely to be a strong influence in your life. Starting with your early childhood you are likely to be curious. If a naturally outgoing child then you are likely to approach adults in your home, family and vicinity with a multitude of questions. If more introverted then you are likely to read books, watch television and explore the world wide web. You learn much from your early home life, preferring the stimulation of an active family. Activity feeds your curious mind. Later in life you replicate this scenario in your own home. You are likely to establish many pastimes within your home, and may even work from home. Whether or not you live on your own, or have a large family, you enjoy a busy household. In some cases this could spill into your career choice. You may choose a profession as a merchant, teacher, writer, researcher, tradesperson, courier or any such job that stimulates your need to make new discoveries inside or outside your own household.

*Mercury Square Moon
You are indecisive, spending much time weighing up the pros and cons. This is because your feelings and thoughts are at odds. As you learn how to compromise you will develop understanding and an inner knowledge on how to act.

*Mercury Square Sun
Mercury is never more than 28 degrees from the Sun so you will only find it listed under conjunctions.

*Mercury Square Venus
Mercury and Venus are never more than 74 degrees from each other so you will only find them listed together under conjunctions and sextiles.

*Mercury Square Mars
You have difficulty concentrating as you have so many thoughts and ideas. You are talkative but lose sight of the essence of the conversation.

*Mercury Square Jupiter
You have many so many ideas and plans that you are not sure which ones to follow. You make promises you can't keep, although your intentions are good.

*Mercury Square Saturn
You become stuck on certain ideas and find it difficult to change your mind. You have difficulty communicating your thoughts to others.

*Mercury Square Uranus
You have so many original thoughts and ideas that you find it difficult to capture them on paper.

*Mercury Square Neptune
You have difficulty using your powers of discrimination. Your own thoughts and opinions are vague and confused and difficult to pin down.

*Mercury Square Pluto
You can be cruel in your speech. You suffer from obsessive thoughts and find it difficult to think positively and calmly. You are focused on your own thoughts and opinions and may not listen to others.

*Mercury Square Chiron
You suffer from believing that you are lacking in intelligence. You have difficulty asserting your own thoughts and opinions. The good news is that you are able to learn from experience. Once you have learnt to value yourself then you are able to share your wisdom with others. You are an excellent listener, carer and counsellor.

*Mercury Square Vesta
Vesta is the Goddess associated with a fire that never goes out. In your case it is combined with the intelligent planet Mercury indicating that you have an equiring mind. It is likely that you have a thirst for knowledge that is hard to quench. You may be drawn to the study of something sacred, such as mathematics, astrology, geometry or mythology. You have a unique talent which needs expression. You may struggle with finding ways in which to express yourself in your younger days, but expressing your ideas gets easier as you mature.

*Mercury Square Juno
The spoken word has a potent effect on your loved ones. When you talk, write, sing or communicate in any manner then you are able to attract a warm and loving audience. However, this is only true if you are speaking kind and loving truth. If you speak harsh words then you may find that you alienate others. Your journey in life is truly blessed with glad tidings when you communicate with love and compassion touching others with your warm and nurturing connections.

*Mercury Square NorthNode
Your communication skills are highly-developed, but you need to avoid your tendency for talk rather than action. You are being challenged to stop scattering your energy in all directions and put your communication skills to good use.

*Mercury Opposition Moon
You struggle to make decisions in your life, unsure whether to follow your feelings or your thoughts; your heart or your head. This means that you doubt yourself much of the time. You need to find a balance between the two.

*Mercury Opposition Sun
Mercury is never more than 28 degrees from the Sun so you will only find it listed under conjunctions.

*Mercury Opposition Venus
Mercury and Venus are never more than 74 degrees from each other so you will only find them listed together under conjunctions and sextiles.

*Mercury Opposition Mars

*Mercury Opposition Jupiter
You are prone to making mountains out of molehills. You struggle to keep a balanced viewpoint, but can become fanatical in pursuit of your beliefs.

*Mercury Opposition Saturn
You have difficulty expressing yourself. As a child you believe your father was critical and judged you lacking in intelligence. As an adult you have trouble believing in your ability to communicate and stand up for your own beliefs.

*Mercury Opposition Uranus
You have a tendency to thrust your own original thoughts and ideas onto other people. You wilfully defend your right to have different views and can fail to appreciate other people's points of view. You need to learn to respect all forms of communication and thinking.

*Mercury Opposition Neptune
You have a tendency to be seduced into believing other people's ideas. You are confused in your own thinking and can be deceived.

*Mercury Opposition Pluto
You have a tendency to become obsessed with your own ideas which you relentlessly impress on others.

*Mercury Opposition Chiron
You suffer from feelings of intellectual inadequacy and believe that other people are better than you. As you face your pain you may become a spokesperson for other wounded people.

*Mercury Opposition Vesta

*Mercury Quincunx Chiron

*Mercury Quincunx Juno
Sometimes you may feel that your words are not having the affect that you would like on those around you. You want to nurture family, friends and colleagues but the words just don't come easily. You may find it difficult to comfort others in troubled times, or perhaps your efforts to communicate are not received in the manner in which you intended. The good news is that you can persist. You can master the art of listening, saying the right thing at the right time and communicating your opinion effectively.

*Mercury Semisquare Chiron
Do you sometimes suffer from "foot in mouth" disease? This is because you have not learnt to pause and consider your own and other people's opinions before you speak. Perhaps someone was mentally cruel to you as a youngster, or perhaps the absence of a key caregiver meant that you did not learn social graces. The good news is that you can learn to think before you speak, to consider other people's points of view and to listen carefully. One of your life lesson's is to learn to listen to others.

*Venus Conjunction Moon
You are calm and gentle and enjoy the company of close friends. You like to surround yourself with beauty. You are drawn to art, music, nature, and spiritual pursuits.

*Venus Conjunction Sun
You are gentle, loving and charming. You express yourself in an affectionate manner and enjoy the company of other people. You also have a love of art and beauty. You can be idealistic and easily hurt.

*Venus Conjunction Mercury
You express yourself in a loving manner. You enjoy talking with people, and they find you a warm and welcoming listener.

*Venus Conjunction Mars
You are charming and assertive, passionate and alive. You love to share your adventures with loved ones, sometimes pushing them reluctantly in front. You have high expectations and can sometimes be disappointed in intimate relationships.

*Venus Conjunction Jupiter
You are fun loving, generous and popular. You know how to indulge yourself and your loved ones. You love to share adventures and philosophies. You love goals. You could be a teacher, travel agent or public relations manager. You need to make sure that your behaviour does not become over-indulgent or extravagant.

*Venus Conjunction Saturn
You are shy and inhibited in your personal relationships. You fear commitment and tend to either be the one in control or to choose a partner who tries to control you. One of your parents may have been too strict and consequently you fear expressing yourself. Once you overcome your feelings of inadequacy you will have the ability to form secure and long-lasting relationships based on firm foundations. You are faithful and loyal.

*Venus Conjunction Uranus
You are determined to be recognised as an individual within your personal relationships. You will not allow anyone to curb your sense of freedom. You tend to get bored and restless in traditional relationships. You want fun, spontaneity and intellectual stimulation from your partners.

*Venus Conjunction Neptune
You yearn for romance within your personal relationships. You are seeking an ideal and perfect partner, who only exists in fairy tales. You become disillusioned with the imperfections of relationships and seek solace in a fantasy world. You need to face the realities and imperfections of yourself and others. Then you will be able to share beauty, art and creative pursuits with your partners.

*Venus Conjunction Pluto
You want intensity and drama in your personal relationships.  You are consumed with love and passion and expect your partner to feel the same way. You are disappointed when others fail to soar to great emotional heights and plummet the emotional depths by your side. On a more positive note you are fiercely loyal and committed with an ability to fight any injustice.

*Venus Conjunction Chiron
You have a childlike innocence in  your personal relationships, which makes you vulnerable to emotional pain. You fear commitment and rejection. You may experience pain in early relationships, but this pain is usually healed giving you insight and wisdom in later personal relationships. You see the beauty in people who have been cast aside by others, and develop the ability to be a teacher or healer in intimate relationships.

*Venus Conjunction Vesta
Vesta is considered a highly sacred Goddess. In your Birth Chart she is influencing the positive planet Venus. This means that beauty, design and pleasure are likely to be  important components of your life, and your key relationships. You are able to attract positive relationships, in some cases sacred ones. Your home and hearth are sources of comfort for your loved ones. You may have a unique artistic talent, but it is more likely that your talent is for forming lasting and meaningful relationships.

*Venus Conjunction Juno
This is a powerfully feminine combination. Whether in a man or woman's Birth Chart this combination of two potent Goddesses indicates a love of women. Actress Mae West has this connection in her Birth Chart. She epitomises a woman who is voluptuous, feminine and feisty. Mae West is also no shrinking violet. This combination means that you are likely to love passionately and earnestly.  As Mae herself said: "A woman in love can't be reasonable - or she probably wouldn't be in love." This is true for both men and women. You nurture your relationships with people, and possibly also with money. Those around you know that you have an impact wherever you go. Relationships are likely to be a priority in your life.

*Venus Conjunction Ceres
When the planet of love Venus combines with Ceres in a harmonious way then your ability to express love and affection is in sync with your nurturing nature. This means that you have a great deal of love and compassion for anyone with whom you are in relationship. Peace, beauty and love feature in your life. You need to make sure that you are not giving more than you receive, as you find it so easy to understand and show compassion to others, particularly your female friends and your lover/s. Make sure that you enjoy social gatherings, sojourns into nature and personal beauty treatments. These nurture your soul.

*Venus Conjunction NorthNode
Your destiny is linked with the need to develop harmonious and balanced relationships. Relationships will play an important role in your accomplishments. You need to make sure that your need to keep the peace does not hinder decisive action.

*Venus Conjunction SouthNode
You have experienced a heavy emphasis on relationships in past lives, which is somehow curtailed in this life. Your difficulties in personal relationships are a sign that you need to focus on your personal relating skills.

*Venus Conjunction Ascendant
You are a warm and attractive person, with an urge to be involved in relationships. Other people will be attracted by your charm. Art and creativity may also play an important role in your life.

*Venus Conjunction Midheaven
You are a charming and soothing person, able to use your charm to help both yourself and other people on life's journey. You believe in co-operation, not competition, and therefore you are an asset in any profession that requires teamwork, personnel skills and diplomacy. You may excel in an artistic field, but this depends on other influences in your birth chart. You are likely to enjoy any work that pays well while enabling you to express your love of people. Relationships are important to you. You are likely  to be benefit from your association with a woman, whether this is in your profession or in marriage. You need to avoid any career that involves conflict, as you are likely to be agitated when trouble arises in the workplace. You are likely to feel the need to escape to calmer work environs when trouble is afoot at work. While generally you land on your feet when it comes to seeking new jobs, you may also benefit from learning some self-soothing techniques, or indulging in an enjoyable pastime that helps alleviate any temporary work stress. While you can excel at any chosen profession you may be attracted to the arts, beauty, fashion, graphic design, leisure, hospitality, or public relations, to name a few.

*Venus Conjunction Imum Coeli

If you live alone then you are likely to find a house that reflects your need for tranquility and creativity. If you share your home with other family members, then you like to ensure that everyone is having a good time. You are the peacemaker, the diplomat and a loving member of any household. You enjoy relating to your family and friends, and making sure that they are at peace with themselves. Any conflict is likely to be upsetting. Sometimes you can sit on the fence when it comes to family politics, but you prefer this to becoming embroiled in other people's problems. You want fun, creativity and harmony. Your personal interests may reflect these qualities. You may possess beautiful artifacts, and artistic talents to complement your charming disposition. These are potent qualities. Your main profession does not necessarily reflect your artistic or personal gifts, however; you are likely to express them in some public arena. For instance your day job may be a practical one that earns you good money, however; at night you revel in amateur arts organisations. Your main job may be as a homemaker but you enjoy demonstrating at cosmetic or fashion parties and earning extra money at night. The most important thing for you is having a sense of peace in your private life.

*Venus Square Saturn

*Venus Square Uranus

*Venus Square Neptune

*Venus Square Pluto

*Venus Square Chiron

*Venus Square Vesta
Vesta is considered a highly sacred Goddess. In your Birth Chart she is influencing the positive planet Venus. This means that women, beauty, design and pleasure are likely to be important components of your life, and your key relationships. You are able to attract positive relationships, in some cases sacred ones, but you do have to work at it.  Women, the role of women in society, and women in the hearth and home are themes that are likely to shine in your life. Your home and hearth are sources of comfort for your loved ones. You are likely to be a powerful force in your own life, but it is also possible that there is a powerful woman or women who spark your passion.

*Venus Square Juno
This combination means that you are likely to love passionately and earnestly.  As American actress Mae West once said: "A woman in love can't be reasonable - or she probably wouldn't be in love." This is true for both men and women. Your ardour is strong once aroused. Even when you are not in love with one person, you nurture your relationships with loved ones, and possibly also with money. Those around you know that you have an impact wherever you go. You need to ensure that you show some restraint when it comes to your own passions.

*Venus Opposition Moon
You experience conflict  between your needs and the needs of other people. This can also mean that you are uncomfortable in social situations. Finding a balance may prove difficult but will mean greater understanding of the give and take needed in relationships.

*Venus Opposition Sun
Venus is never more than 46 degrees from the Sun so you will only find it listed under conjunctions.

*Venus Opposition Mercury
Mercury and Venus are never more than 74 degrees from each other so you will only find them listed together under conjunctions and sextiles.

*Venus Opposition Mars
You struggle to balance your own needs and the needs of your partners in relationships. You see-saw between wanting closeness and freedom. On the one hand you seek adventure on your own, on the other you want to be close to your partner. The ideal is a balance between the two.

*Venus Opposition Jupiter
You are a social climber. You grapple with extravagance, wastefulness and a child-like expectancy that someone will come to your rescue. Your conflict is that you have become dependent on other people and have forgotten how to stand on your own. The lesson is moderation.

*Venus Opposition Saturn
You have an inability to trust and show your love for other people. This probably stems from childhood experiences with your parents. You may have felt unworthy of your parents' love. Alternatively you may have perceived your parents' as cold and unloving. As an adult you may become involved in relationships with an older person or someone who offers you financial or emotional security. You need to develop your own value system and develop compassion for yourself and other people.

*Venus Opposition Uranus
You are torn between a need to be loved in an intimate relationship and a desire to be your own person. You are wilful in your desire for freedom and find it difficult to commit yourself to one relationship. You need to develop an appreciation for your own and others' unique talents.

*Venus Opposition Neptune
Conflict arises in your personal relationships because of your lack of discernment. You are caught in a web of fantasies and romantic illusions and become easily deceived in your close relationships. You need to find a creative outlet for your imagination.

*Venus Opposition Pluto
Drama plays a key role in your personal relationships. You are obsessed with the concept of love and desire and expect your loved ones to share your intensity. Your relationships are strewn with struggles for power and control, and possibly violence. You need to direct your energies into a demanding, creative pursuit.

You also tend to become the peacemaker as you are so sensitive to disharmony. You need to learn to nurture yourself and trust your own wisdom.

*Mars Conjunction NorthNode

*Mars Conjunction SouthNode
You are a compulsive person, liable to act before you think. This can lead you into hot water, particularly when you act independently without taking other people into consideration. One of your life lessons is to curb this compulsive behaviour, to think before you act and to find a way to express your own goals positively and co-operatively. You do have a stubborn streak which may have served you well at some time in your early life, but it does not augur well for adult relationships. Like an only child who is accustomed to getting all that he or she wants in life, you need to remind yourself of the rights of others. This will encourage your talent for independent action while also auguring well for co-operative and supportive interactions.  Assertion not agression is the key to your success.

*Mars Conjunction Ascendant

*Mars Conjunction Midheaven
Self-confidence plays a vital role in how you handle your professional life. If you had a stable and loving home life, as depicted in other aspects of your birth chart, then you are likely to stride forth into the world with confidence. You set your goals, work steadily towards achieving them and then enjoy your success in any chosen profession. Of course sports, politics, and law may feature. On the other hand if you lack self-confidence then you may falter in your chosen career. You may start with the very best of intentions, setting your goals and moving forward. However, any obstacles or conflict may upset your course. As a result you could suffer from stress-related illnesses at the sign of any professional setback.  You may also make rash decisions which adversely affect your advancement in life. If this is the case then you need to seek professional advice either through personal counseling, vocational guidance or some other such course of action that helps you build your esteem, make wise choices and achieve the success that you so desire. *Mars Conjunction Imum Coeli

Once you have chosen one place in which to nest, then you need plenty of activity within your house. You may share with many people, or perhaps you could develop some robust home activities such as renovation projects or a home gym. You need an outlet for your boundless energy, as well as a respect for the fact that other household members may require a quieter existence. If you are bored you can be quite the agitator, annoying those around you. Therefore some home activities that demand your energy can be therapeutic for everyone.

The serious planet Saturn is in a significant position in your birth chart suggesting that family responsibilities need to be attended to before you can succeed in the public world. This can mean that some serious childhood matters need to be faced and dealt with before you can move forward on your own life's journey. Perhaps these matters are connected to your father, or your father's family. Your early family life may not have been as supportive as you would have liked, resulting in you feeling a lack of a firm footing.  In some cases it could be that your family life was generally secure but that your parents moved house, forcing you to begin again in a new environment and creating a sense of insecurity. While some children adapt well to new homes and neighbourhoods, you had difficulty coping with the changes. As you grow and mature you find that you've to come to terms with these early difficulties. Gradually you learn how to build up a solid foundation that suits you and your home life becomes a solid base for you and you are ready to branch out and secure a future through your profession, or through marriage and a family of your own. The ancient prophets believed that this was a highly significant placement for the planet Saturn and therefore you are likely to have learnt some valuable lessons. Perhaps you realise that there is no point in holding on to the past but rather to focus on the foundations of the present moment.

*Neptune Conjunction Imum Coeli
