Your challenge is to assert your own rights within your family without resorting to aggression, or without becoming the victim of someone else's aggressive behaviour or perpetuating any trauma. Your childhood experiences can be a source of wisdom as you mature, enabling you to form a strong foundation in your own life, and for family members. This placement can also influence your choice of career. For this reason you may work in a field such as psychology, aged care, real estate, or politics.

Early childhood is not always easy with this placement of Chiron. Your family life does not support your true self. This may be linked to your relationship with your father, rather than your mother. Perhaps you feel rejected, or neglected, by your father? You are likely to repeat this pattern until you can find a place in which you truly belong, somewhere deep inside yourself that feels safe. Once this occurs then you can form a home, and family environment, that is secure and loving. You are likely to then be a loving and healing presence in your family.

*Chiron Opposition Moon
Within you exists a deep emotional pain stemming originally from your relationship with your mother. You attract partners and situations which reflect that pain. It may be that your partner needs much caring or it may be that your partner sparks your wounds. The lesson is to face the pain and learn to balance your needs with the needs of others. You may then become a wise and loving healer.

*Chiron Opposition Sun
You have difficulty shining in your life because of a childhood wound, perhaps connected with your father. You  lack confidence and feel lonely at times. Nevertheless this very wound is the source of great understanding, and gives you a unique strength to help yourself, and others. You have much empathy for other people's suffering and may become a healer or counsellor.

*Chiron Opposition Mercury
You suffer from feelings of intellectual inadequacy and believe that other people are better than you. As you face your pain you may become a spokesperson for other wounded people.

*Chiron Opposition Venus
You tend to suffer emotional pain in your personal relationships. You are so busy caring for your loved ones that you neglect your own needs. This imbalance can lead to you resenting your partners . You also tend to become the peacemaker as you are so sensitive to disharmony. You need to learn to nurture yourself and trust your own wisdom.

*Chiron Opposition Mars
You are your own worst enemy. You struggle to be powerful and assertive, but your path to success is strewn with strife. This may have started early in life when your home felt more like a battlefield than a safe haven leaving you feeling powerless and ineffective. Now it appears that other people are opposed to your achievements. What you don't realise is that you are subconsciously sabotaging your own success. You need to honor your own and other people's worth. You may find that the battle then becomes one which you lead for those who need your empathy and help.

*Chiron Opposition Jupiter
The fact that other people do not live up to your high ideals causes you pain. At times your emotional pain may even seem unbearable. You have such high hopes for humanity. You may struggle with orthodox religion or become a religious fanatic. Your lesson is to find the answers within. You may find that dedicating yourself to an appropriate cause helps you find a balance in your life.  Take time to reflect on your experiences. Your insights may lead to wisdom.

*Chiron Opposition Saturn
You struggle with authority and restrictions in your life. As a child your father may have been absent or overly strict. As a result you fear rejection and suffer from bouts of hopelessness. You may attract partners who repeat this childhood pattern. You need to face your emotional pain in a disciplined manner in order to discover your own natural sense of authority and wisdom.

*Chiron Opposition Uranus
This opposition is common between approximately 1952 and 1989 and therefore has a generational effect. On a personal level: You have a wilful desire for freedom, and are likely to cut ties and to make sudden changes if circumstances or people stand in your way. Your strong desire to express your freedom may be as a result of your inability to face deep emotional wounds. Your task is to honor your intuition and foresight and find a creative outlet for your unique talents. This combination also gives you a sensitivity to esoteric matters. As such you may be drawn to metaphysical matters, cutting-edge ideas and supporting fringe dwellers in society.

*Chiron Opposition Neptune
You struggle to live in the real world. You see the world as a dangerous place from which you would like to escape. You may become drawn into the world of drugs or alcohol, or escape through fantasies. You may also suffer from ill health. Your lesson is to express the sensitive and caring side of your nature in a spiritually constructive way.

*Chiron Opposition Pluto
You struggle with the darker side of life feeling overcome by passions such as envy, greed, lust, and jealousy. You do not understand from where these destructive thoughts emerge, but are aware that the more you try to push them to one side the more they grow in magnitude. Your lesson is to delve into your past, recognise past feelings of rejection, and to transform your newfound understanding into positive outlets. You may become a powerful healer, or attract powerful healers into your own life.

*Chiron Opposition NorthNode

*Chiron Opposition Imum Coeli
Do you ever feel like the odd one out in your chosen profession? You are talking but no one else listens? Perhaps you wonder why you are the one who is always overlooked for a promotion? This is because you are different - in a good way. You are a prophet in your own profession, but your skills are not necessarily of an imminently practical nature. Therefore other people don't immediately see the measure of your worth. This can be painful, particularly if events or people trigger subconscious recollections of rejection by your parents. It is possible that your mother, or both parents, did not listen to you or encourage your choices. At school you may have been encourage to study subjects that were not suited to your talents. As a result you felt lost, unable to achieve, when really all you needed was to take a different path. Your initial career choice may not reflect your true purpose. Hence you still feel like a fish out of water. Eventually a light switches on and one of two things can happen. You begin to value your own worth within your current occupation, or you change career paths. Healing, spirituality, and any of the feminine arts may suit you professionally. No matter what your career, you bring much wisdom to your chosen profession. Once you accept an alternative career, or a different attitude then doors open and you receive the recognition that you truly need. Ironically this recognition may not come from other people but from a deep sense of satisfaction that you are on the right path.

*Chiron Semisquare Sun

*Chiron Semisquare Mercury
Do you sometimes suffer from "foot in mouth" disease? This is because you have not learnt to pause and consider your own and other people's opinions before you speak. Perhaps someone was mentally cruel to you as a youngster, or perhaps the absence of a key caregiver meant that you did not learn social graces. The good news is that you can learn to think before you speak, to consider other people's points of view and to listen carefully. One of your life lesson's is to learn to listen to others.

*Vesta Conjunction Sun
Vesta is the Goddess associated with the sacred matters related to everyday functions. She depicts the rituals of work and wellbeing. This Goddess is combining with your Sun Sign to suggest that your own well being is of vital importance. You need to ensure that you maintain a healthy sense of self-esteem and look after your self. Daily rituals such as yoga, meditation and exercise are likely to be highly beneficial. 

*Vesta Conjunction Mercury
Vesta is the Goddess associated with a fire that never goes out. In your case it is combined with the intelligent planet Mercury indicating that you have an equiring mind. It is likely that you have a thirst for knowledge that is hard to quench. You may be drawn to the study of something sacred, such as mathematics, astrology, geometry or mythology.  Whatever your choice of topic, you are likely to excel because you have an intellectual spark that is equal to none. Your intellect is unique. 

*Vesta Conjunction Venus
Vesta is considered a highly sacred Goddess. In your Birth Chart she is influencing the positive planet Venus. This means that beauty, design and pleasure are likely to be  important components of your life, and your key relationships. You are able to attract positive relationships, in some cases sacred ones. Your home and hearth are sources of comfort for your loved ones. You may have a unique artistic talent, but it is more likely that your talent is for forming lasting and meaningful relationships.

*Vesta Conjunction Mars
When you have this combination you need to ensure that you discover what lights your fire and never let the passion fade. You are destined to direct your energies into something sacred, an activity, project or profession that inspires others. A woman, or group of women, may provide you with the encouragement that you need, but you also need to fan the flames.

*Vesta Conjunction Saturn
This astrological combination can indicate a leader, someone who can build a team of workers or a strong family unit. If you believe in something then you can move mountains. Contrarily if you are not committed then you are bored and move on to something more worthwhile. You know the true worth of hard work and are happy to work with others who share this value, but you do not suffer fools easily. You are the type of person who is likely to achieve much later in life by nurturing your own talents and beliefs, and those of other people. You earn the respect of those around you through the longevity and application of your personal values in whatever you do. 

*Vesta Conjunction Uranus
This combination indicates that you are able to see beyond yourself, that you are genuinely concerned for the plight of humanity and those less fortunate. You may have strong spiritual convictions. These are unlikely to be conventional. Other people may consult you for guidance. You need to be careful of caring more for your causes and for others, rather than for yourself. You are an expert in your field, but you are not the only person who can help.

*Pallas Conjunction Moon
The Olympian goddess Pallas Athena was a daughter of Zeus, born from her father's head after he had swallowed Metis. The Romans referred to her as Minerva. She is revered as representing the wisdom of reflection and strategy. When combined with the Moon in your chart she emphasises your instinctive need to retreat and formulate a plan before making any emotional leaps of faith. You are a born strategist. 

*Pallas Conjunction Mars
Adventure is likely to have an influence on your relationships. This can mean that you are an independent person who needs an equally independent partner or that you need plenty of freedom to assert yourself in partnerships. You are likely to be assertive in your partnerships, unafraid of confrontation. You may venture into relationships that are not conducive to your own wellbeing and safety. Therefore you need to carefully vet any potentional partner. Also even though you do not fear conflict, you would be well advised to avoid it where possible. Issues of equality, fidelity and traditional roles within relationships are important to you.

*Pallas Conjunction Pluto
You have the ability to be both practical and creative. If you have musical or artistic talent you can give it form and make something long lasting. You are prepared to put in the practice needed to perfect your creative talents. You may be a performer.

*Pallas Square Pluto
You lack confidence in your artistic ability or in your relationships. Learn to believe in yourself and avoid being drawn into the psychic realms as you still have to learn how to deal with the practical side of life.

Of course you may choose your own independent path, rather than a domestic shared arrangement.

*Juno Conjunction Moon

*Juno Conjunction Sun

You are likely to express yourself best when in relationship with other people. Diplomacy and fairness are likely to be traits that you value. *Juno Conjunction Mercury

This can be a positive trait if you are sensitive and loving in your communications. However, any harsh words are likely to be amplified. You must be just, calm and caring when communicating with others. *Ceres Conjunction Moon
The Roman goddess Ceres is also known as Olympian goddess, Demeter. She is the mother of Persephone. She is the Corn Goddess who personifies the agricultural cycle of fertility and harvest, as well as loss and renewal through her daughter Persephone. Therefore you are likely to have a close relationship with women and an affinity with nature and Mother Earth. You are a born nurturer longing to tend to the needs of others and happy as long as you and your loved ones are feeling ok. You understand the cycles of life, and the undercurrents of relations between women. It is possible that your home is one that is predominantly filled with women. On the other hand you may surround yourself with female co-workers, friends and relatives. You are happiest when you are intimately involved in the lives of others.

*Ceres Conjunction Sun

You need to make sure that you are not giving more than you receive, as you find it so easy to understand and show compassion to others, particularly your female friends and your lover/s. Make sure that you enjoy social gatherings, sojourns into nature and personal beauty treatments. These nurture your soul.

For this reason you may stand out from the crowd. Others may rely on you to speak up on their behalf. You are a leader rather than a follower.

You need a marriage that gives you just the right amount of freedom to pursue your independent activities. It is best if you are cautious before making a commitment, ensuring that your partner has the same need for freedom as you. Then you can create a unique union which is lively, interactive and certainly never boring.
